</span>\n            </li>\n            <li>\n             <span class="noprint">\n              <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Sandy_in_New_York" title="Effects of Hurricane Sandy in New </span>\n         </p>\n         <ul>\n          <li>\n           <span class="noprint">\n            <a class="extiw" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:Hurricane_Sandy_(2012)" title="commons:Category:Hurricane Sandy (2012)">\n             Commons: Sandy images\n            </a>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n          <li>\n           <span class="noprint">\n            <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikinews.org/wiki/Category:Hurricane_Sandy" title="wikinews:Category:Hurricane Sandy">\n             Wikinews: Sandy stories\n            </a>\n           </span>\n          </li>\n         </ul>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <b>\n        Hurricane Sandy\n       </b>\n       (unofficially referred to as "Superstorm Sandy")\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-not_The_Big_One_1-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-not_The_Big_One-1">\n         [1]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Superstorm_Sandy_Anniversary_2-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Superstorm_Sandy_Anniversary-2">\n         [2]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       was the deadliest and most destructive\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone" title="Tropical cyclone">\n        hurricane\n       </a>\n       of the\n       <a href="/wiki/2012_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2012 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        2012 Atlantic hurricane season\n       </a>\n       , and the third-costliest hurricane in United States history.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Classified as the eighteenth\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclone_naming" title="Tropical cyclone naming">\n        named storm\n       </a>\n       , tenth\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hurricane" title="Hurricane">\n        hurricane\n       </a>\n       and second\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Major_hurricane" title="Major hurricane">\n        major hurricane\n       </a>\n       of the year, Sandy was a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_hurricane_wind_scale#Category_3" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson hurricane wind scale">\n        Category 3\n       </a>\n       storm at its peak intensity when it made landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cuba" title="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       While it was a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_Hurricane_Scale#Category_2" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson Hurricane Scale">\n        Category 2\n       </a>\n       hurricane off the coast of the Northeastern United States, the storm became the largest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Atlantic_tropical_cyclone" title="North Atlantic tropical cyclone">\n        Atlantic hurricane\n       </a>\n       on record (as measured by diameter, with winds spanning 1,100 miles (1,800\xc2\xa0km)).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-4">\n         [4]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-5">\n         [5]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Estimates as of 2015 assessed damage to have been about $75 billion (2012\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/USD" title="USD">\n        USD\n       </a>\n       ), a total surpassed only by hurricanes\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n        Katrina\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Harvey" title="Hurricane Harvey">\n        Harvey\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyServAssess0513_6-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyServAssess0513-6">\n         [6]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At least 233 people were killed along the path of the storm in eight countries.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diakakis_et_al_2013_7-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Diakakis_et_al_2013-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-8">\n         [8]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Sandy developed from a\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_wave" title="Tropical wave">\n        tropical wave\n       </a>\n       in the western Caribbean Sea on October\xc2\xa022, quickly strengthened, and was upgraded to Tropical Storm Sandy six hours later. Sandy moved slowly northward toward the\n       <a href="/wiki/Greater_Antilles" title="Greater Antilles">\n        Greater Antilles\n       </a>\n       and gradually intensified. On October 24, Sandy became a hurricane, made landfall near\n       <a href="/wiki/Kingston,_Jamaica" title="Kingston, Jamaica">\n        Kingston, Jamaica\n       </a>\n       , re-emerged a few hours later into the Caribbean Sea and strengthened into a Category 2 hurricane. On October 25, Sandy hit Cuba as a Category 3 hurricane, then weakened to a Category 1 hurricane. Early on October 26, Sandy moved through the Bahamas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-9">\n         [9]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 27, Sandy briefly weakened to a tropical storm and then restrengthened to a Category\xc2\xa01 hurricane. Early on October\xc2\xa029, Sandy curved west-northwest (the "left turn" or "left hook") and then\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-10">\n         [10]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       moved ashore near\n       <a href="/wiki/Brigantine,_New_Jersey" title="Brigantine, New Jersey">\n        Brigantine, New Jersey\n       </a>\n       , just to the northeast of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Atlantic_City" title="Atlantic City">\n        Atlantic City\n       </a>\n       , as a\n       <a href="/wiki/Post-tropical_cyclone" title="Post-tropical cyclone">\n        post-tropical cyclone\n       </a>\n       with hurricane-force winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-11">\n         [11]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">\n        Jamaica\n       </a>\n       , winds left 70% of residents without electricity, blew roofs off buildings, killed one, and caused about $100\xc2\xa0million (2012\xc2\xa0USD) in damage. Sandy\'s outer bands brought flooding to\n       <a href="/wiki/Haiti" title="Haiti">\n        Haiti\n       </a>\n       , killing at least 54, causing food shortages, and leaving about 200,000 homeless; the hurricane also caused two deaths in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       . In\n       <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">\n        Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       , one man was swept away by a swollen river. In Cuba, there was extensive coastal flooding and wind damage inland, destroying some 15,000 homes, killing 11, and causing $2\xc2\xa0billion (2012\xc2\xa0USD) in damage. Sandy caused two deaths and damage estimated at $700\xc2\xa0million (2012\xc2\xa0USD) in\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Bahamas" title="The Bahamas">\n        The Bahamas\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the United States, Hurricane Sandy affected 24\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">\n        states\n       </a>\n       , including the entire eastern seaboard from\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">\n        Florida\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">\n        Maine\n       </a>\n       and west across the\n       <a href="/wiki/Appalachian_Mountains" title="Appalachian Mountains">\n        Appalachian Mountains\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">\n        Michigan\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Wisconsin" title="Wisconsin">\n        Wisconsin\n       </a>\n       , with particularly severe damage in\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">\n        New York\n       </a>\n       . Its\n       <a href="/wiki/Storm_surge" title="Storm surge">\n        storm surge\n       </a>\n       hit\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">\n        New York City\n       </a>\n       on October 29, flooding streets, tunnels and subway lines and cutting power in and around the city.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-12">\n         [12]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-13">\n         [13]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage in the United States amounted to $71.4\xc2\xa0billion (2013 USD).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AOMLCostliest_14-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AOMLCostliest-14">\n         [14]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Canada, two were killed in Ontario and an estimated $100 million (\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadian_dollar" title="Canadian dollar">\n        2012 CAD\n       </a>\n       ) in damage was caused throughout Ontario and Quebec.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">\n        <a href="#cite_note-15">\n         [15]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="toclimit-4">\n       <div class="toc" id="toc">\n        <div class="toctitle">\n         <h2>\n          Contents\n         </h2>\n        </div>\n        <ul>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 <ul>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-47">\n            <a href="#Relief_efforts">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              4.1\n             </span>\n             <span    <a href="#Baby_boom">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              4.6\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Baby boom\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-53">\n            <a href="#Retirement_of_the_name">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              4.7\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              Retirement of the name\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n           <li class="toclevel-2 tocsection-54">\n            <a href="#In_popular_culture">\n             <span class="tocnumber">\n              4.8\n             </span>\n             <span class="toctext">\n              In popular culture\n             </span>\n            </a>\n           </li>\n          </ul>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-55">\n          <a href="#See_also">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            5\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            See also\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-56">\n          <a href="#References">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            6\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            References\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </li>\n         <li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-57">\n          <a href="#External_links">\n           <span class="tocnumber">\n            7\n           </span>\n           <span class="toctext">\n            External links\n           </span>\n          </a>\n         </li>\n        </ul>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Meteorological_history">\n        Meteorological history\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Meteorological_history_of_Hurricane_Sandy" title="Meteorological history of Hurricane Sandy">\n        Meteorological history of Hurricane Sandy\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sandy_2012_track.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2334" data-file-width="2700" height="190" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Sandy_2012_track.png/220px-Sandy_2012_track.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Sandy_2012_track.png/330px-Sandy_2012_track.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/92/Sandy_2012_track.png/440px-Sandy_2012_track.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sandy_2012_track.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Map plotting the track and intensity of the storm, according to the\n         <a href="/wiki/Saffir%E2%80%93Simpson_scale" title="Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale">\n          Saffir\xe2\x80\x93Simpson scale\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Sandy began as a low pressure system which developed sufficient organized\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Convection_(meteorology)" title="Convection (meteorology)">\n        convection\n       </a>\n       to be classified as Tropical Depression Eighteen on October\xc2\xa022 south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Kingston,_Jamaica" title="Kingston, Jamaica">\n        Kingston, Jamaica\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-disc1_16-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-disc1-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It moved slowly at first due to a\n       <a href="/wiki/Ridge_(meteorology)" title="Ridge (meteorology)">\n        ridge\n       </a>\n       to the north. Low\n       <a href="/wiki/Wind_shear" title="Wind shear">\n        wind shear\n       </a>\n       and warm\n       <a href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperature" title="Sea surface temperature">\n        waters\n       </a>\n       allowed for strengthening,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-disc1_16-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-disc1-16">\n         [16]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the system was\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Atlantic_hurricane_naming_list" title="North Atlantic hurricane naming list">\n        named\n       </a>\n       Tropical Storm Sandy late on October\xc2\xa022.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17">\n        <a href="#cite_note-17">\n         [17]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on October\xc2\xa024, an\n       <a href="/wiki/Eye_(cyclone)" title="Eye (cyclone)">\n        eye\n       </a>\n       began developing, and it was moving steadily northward due to an approaching\n       <a href="/wiki/Trough_(meteorology)" title="Trough (meteorology)">\n        trough\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">\n        <a href="#cite_note-18">\n         [18]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Later that day, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center (NHC)\n       </a>\n       upgraded Sandy to hurricane status about 65\xc2\xa0mi (105\xc2\xa0km) south of Kingston, Jamaica.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-19">\n        <a href="#cite_note-19">\n         [19]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At about 1900\xc2\xa0UTC that day, Sandy made\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Landfall_(meteorology)" title="Landfall (meteorology)">\n        landfall\n       </a>\n       near Kingston with winds of about 85\xc2\xa0mph (140\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20">\n        <a href="#cite_note-20">\n         [20]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Just offshore Cuba, Sandy rapidly intensified to winds of 115\xc2\xa0mph (185\xc2\xa0km/h),\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and at that intensity it made landfall just west of\n       <a href="/wiki/Santiago_de_Cuba" title="Santiago de Cuba">\n        Santiago de Cuba\n       </a>\n       at 0525\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa025.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">\n        <a href="#cite_note-21">\n         [21]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_0" <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_sandy_nasa_satelite_time_lapse_video.ogv" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A time-lapse video made from NASA satellite images of Hurricane Sandy\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       After Sandy exited Cuba, the structure became disorganized,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">\n        <a href="#cite_note-22">\n         [22]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and it turned to the north-northwest over the Bahamas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-23">\n        <a href="#cite_note-23">\n         [23]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By October\xc2\xa027, Sandy was no longer fully tropical, and despite strong shear, it maintained convection due to influence from an approaching trough; the same trough turned the hurricane to the northeast.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-24">\n        <a href="#cite_note-24">\n         [24]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After briefly weakening to a tropical storm,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-25">\n        <a href="#cite_note-25">\n         [25]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Sandy re-intensified into a hurricane,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-26">\n        <a href="#cite_note-26">\n         [26]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and on October\xc2\xa028 an eye began redeveloping.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-27">\n        <a href="#cite_note-27">\n         [27]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm moved around an\n       <a href="/wiki/Cold-core_low" title="Cold-core low">\n        upper-level low\n       </a>\n       over the eastern United States and also to the southwest of a ridge over\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Canada" title="Atlantic Canada">\n        Atlantic Canada\n       </a>\n       , turning it to the northwest.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-disc28_28-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-disc28-28">\n         [28]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Sandy briefly re-intensified to Category 2 intensity on the morning of October\xc2\xa029, around which time it had a wind diameter of over 1,150\xc2\xa0miles (1,850\xc2\xa0km), and a central pressure of 943 mb, which set records for many cities across the\n       <a href="/wiki/Northeastern_United_States" title="Northeastern United States">\n        Northeastern United States\n       </a>\n       for the lowest\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Barometric_pressure" title="Barometric pressure">\n        pressures\n       </a>\n       ever observed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-29">\n        <a href="#cite_note-29">\n         [29]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The convection diminished while the hurricane accelerated toward the New Jersey coast,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-30">\n        <a href="#cite_note-30">\n         [30]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and the hurricane was no longer tropical by 2100\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa029.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-31">\n        <a href="#cite_note-31">\n         [31]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       About 2\n       <sup>\n        1\n       </sup>\n       /\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       hours later, Sandy made landfall near Brigantine, New Jersey,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-32">\n        <a href="#cite_note-32">\n         [32]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with winds of 80\xc2\xa0mph (130\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the next four days, Sandy\'s remnants drifted northward and then northeastward over\n       <a href="/wiki/Ontario" title="Ontario">\n        Ontario\n       </a>\n       , before merging with another low pressure area over\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Canada" title="Eastern Canada">\n        Eastern Canada\n       </a>\n       on November 2.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sandy_absorbed_33-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Sandy_absorbed-33">\n         [33]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Forecasts">\n        Forecasts\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On October 23, 2012, the path of Hurricane Sandy was correctly predicted by the\n       <a href="/wiki/European_Centre_for_Medium-Range_Weather_Forecasts" title="European Centre for Medium-Range Weather Forecasts">\n        European Centre for Medium-Range Weather Forecasts\n       </a>\n       (ECMWF) headquartered in\n       <a href="/wiki/Reading,_Berkshire" title="Reading, Berkshire">\n        Reading, England\n       </a>\n       nearly eight days in advance of its striking the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        American East Coast\n       </a>\n       . The computer model noted that the storm would turn west towards land and strike the New York/New Jersey region on October 29, rather than turn east and head out to the open Atlantic as most hurricanes in this position do. By October 27, four days after the ECMWF made its prediction, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Weather_Service" title="National Weather Service">\n        National Weather Service\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       confirmed the path of the hurricane predicted by the European model. The National Weather Service was criticized for not employing its higher-resolution forecast models the way that its European counterpart did. A hardware and software upgrade completed at the end of 2013 enabled the weather service to make more accurate predictions, and do so far more in advance than the technology in 2012 had allowed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-34">\n        <a href="#cite_note-34">\n         [34]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Relation_to_global_warming">\n        Relation to global warming\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_cyclones_and_climate_change" title="Tropical cyclones and climate change">\n        Tropical cyclones and climate change\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       According to\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NCAR" title="NCAR">\n        NCAR\n       </a>\n       senior climatologist\n       <a href="/wiki/Kevin_E._Trenberth" title="Kevin E. Trenberth">\n        Kevin E. Trenberth\n       </a>\n       , "The answer to the oft-asked question of whether an event is caused by\n       <a href="/wiki/Global_warming" title="Global warming">\n        climate change\n       </a>\n       is that it is the wrong question. All weather events are affected by climate change because the environment in which they occur is warmer and moister than it used to be."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-35">\n        <a href="#cite_note-35">\n         [35]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Oceanic_and_Atmospheric_Administration" title="National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration">\n        NOAA\n       </a>\n       meteorologist Martin Hoerling attributes Sandy to "little more than the coincidental alignment of a tropical storm with an extratropical storm",\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Revkin_36-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Revkin-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Trenberth does agree that the storm was caused by "natural variability" but adds that it was "enhanced by global warming".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SurfTemps_37-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SurfTemps-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One factor contributing to the storm\'s strength was abnormally warm\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sea_surface_temperatures" title="Sea surface temperatures">\n        sea surface temperatures\n       </a>\n       offshore the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        East Coast of the United States\n       </a>\n       \xe2\x80\x94more than 3\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C (5\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F) above normal, to which global warming had contributed 0.6\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0C (1\xc2\xa0\xc2\xb0F).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SurfTemps_37-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SurfTemps-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As the temperature of the atmosphere increases, the capacity to hold water increases, leading to stronger storms and higher rainfall amounts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SurfTemps_37-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SurfTemps-37">\n         [37]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As they move north, Atlantic hurricanes typically are forced east and out to sea by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Westerlies" title="Westerlies">\n        Prevailing Westerlies\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Masters_38-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Masters-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In Sandy\'s case, this typical pattern was\n       <a href="/wiki/Block_(meteorology)" title="Block (meteorology)">\n        blocked\n       </a>\n       by a ridge of high pressure over Greenland resulting in a negative\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Atlantic_Oscillation" title="North Atlantic Oscillation">\n        North Atlantic Oscillation\n       </a>\n       , forming a kink in the jet stream, causing it to double back on itself off the East Coast. Sandy was caught up in this northwesterly flow.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Masters_38-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Masters-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The blocking pattern over Greenland also stalled an\n       <a href="/wiki/Arctic_front" title="Arctic front">\n        Arctic front\n       </a>\n       which combined with the cyclone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Masters_38-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Masters-38">\n         [38]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mark Fischetti of\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Scientific_American" title="Scientific American">\n         Scientific American\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       said that the jet stream\'s unusual shape was caused by\n       <a href="/wiki/Climate_change_in_the_Arctic" title="Climate change in the Arctic">\n        the melting of Arctic ice\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-39">\n        <a href="#cite_note-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Trenberth said that while a negative North Atlantic Oscillation and a blocking anticyclone were in place, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Null_hypothesis" title="Null hypothesis">\n        null hypothesis\n       </a>\n       remained that this was just the natural variability of weather.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Revkin_36-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Revkin-36">\n         [36]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Sea level at New York and along the New Jersey coast\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Current_sea_level_rise" title="Current sea level rise">\n        has increased by nearly a foot\n       </a>\n       (300 mm) over the last hundred years,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-40">\n        <a href="#cite_note-40">\n         [40]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which contributed to the\n       <a href="/wiki/Storm_surge" title="Storm surge">\n        storm surge\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-41">\n        <a href="#cite_note-41">\n         [41]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Harvard geologist\n       <a href="/wiki/Daniel_P._Schrag" title="Daniel P. Schrag">\n        Daniel P. Schrag\n       </a>\n       calls Hurricane Sandy\'s 13-foot (4 m) storm surge an example of what will, by mid-century, be the "new norm on the Eastern seaboard".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-42">\n        <a href="#cite_note-42">\n         [42]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Preparations">\n        Preparations\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Caribbean_and_Bermuda">\n        Caribbean and Bermuda\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       After the storm became a tropical cyclone on October 22, the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Jamaica" title="Government of Jamaica">\n        Government of Jamaica\n       </a>\n       issued a tropical storm watch for the entire island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-43">\n        <a href="#cite_note-43">\n         [43]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Early on October\xc2\xa023, the watch was replaced with a tropical storm warning and a hurricane watch was issued.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-44">\n        <a href="#cite_note-44">\n         [44]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At 1500\xc2\xa0UTC, the hurricane watch was upgraded to a hurricane warning, while the tropical storm warning was discontinued.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-advis5_45-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-advis5-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In preparation of the storm, many residents stocked up on supplies and reinforced roofing material. Acting Prime Minister Peter Phillips urged people to take this storm seriously, and also to take care of their neighbors, especially the elderly, children, and disabled. Government officials shut down schools, government buildings, and the airport in Kingston on the day prior to the arrival of Sandy. Meanwhile, numerous and early curfews were put in place to protect residents, properties, and to prevent crime.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-46">\n        <a href="#cite_note-46">\n         [46]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Shortly after Jamaica issued its first watch on October\xc2\xa022, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Government_of_Haiti" title="Government of Haiti">\n        Government of Haiti\n       </a>\n       issued a tropical storm watch for Haiti.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-47">\n        <a href="#cite_note-47">\n         [47]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By late October\xc2\xa023, it was modified to a tropical storm warning.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-48">\n        <a href="#cite_note-48">\n         [48]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_Cuba" title="Government of Cuba">\n        Government of Cuba\n       </a>\n       posted a hurricane watch for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Provinces_of_Cuba" title="Provinces of Cuba">\n        Cuban Provinces\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Camag%C3%BCey_Province" title="Camag\xc3\xbcey Province">\n        Camag\xc3\xbcey\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Granma_Province" title="Granma Province">\n        Granma\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Guant%C3%A1namo_Province" title="Guant\xc3\xa1namo Province">\n        Guant\xc3\xa1namo\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Holgu%C3%ADn_Province" title="Holgu\xc3\xadn Province">\n        Holgu\xc3\xadn\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Las_Tunas_Province" title="Las Tunas Province">\n        Las Tunas\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Santiago_de_Cuba_Province" title="Santiago de Cuba Province">\n        Santiago de Cuba\n       </a>\n       at 1500\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa023.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-advis5_45-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-advis5-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Only three hours later, the hurricane watch was switched to a hurricane warning.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-advis6_49-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-advis6-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Government_of_the_Bahamas" title="Government of the Bahamas">\n        Government of the Bahamas\n       </a>\n       , at 1500\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa023, issued a tropical storm watch for several Bahamian islands, including the\n       <a href="/wiki/Acklins" title="Acklins">\n        Acklins\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Cat_Island,_Bahamas" title="Cat Island, Bahamas">\n        Cat Island\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Crooked_Island,_Bahamas" title="Crooked Island, Bahamas">\n        Crooked Island\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Exuma" title="Exuma">\n        Exuma\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Inagua" title="Inagua">\n        Inagua\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Cay" title="Long Cay">\n        Long Cay\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Island,_Bahamas" title="Long Island, Bahamas">\n        Long Island\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mayaguana" title="Mayaguana">\n        Mayaguana\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ragged_Island,_Bahamas" title="Ragged Island, Bahamas">\n        Ragged Island\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Rum_Cay" title="Rum Cay">\n        Rum Cay\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/San_Salvador_Island" title="San Salvador Island">\n        San Salvador Island\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-advis5_45-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-advis5-45">\n         [45]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Later that day, another tropical storm watch was issued for\n       <a href="/wiki/Abaco_Islands" title="Abaco Islands">\n        Abaco Islands\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Andros,_Bahamas" title="Andros, Bahamas">\n        Andros Island\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Berry_Islands" title="Berry Islands">\n        Berry Islands\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bimini" title="Bimini">\n        Bimini\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Eleuthera" title="Eleuthera">\n        Eleuthera\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Grand_Bahama" title="Grand Bahama">\n        Grand Bahama\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Providence" title="New Providence">\n        New Providence\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-advis6_49-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-advis6-49">\n         [49]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By early on October\xc2\xa024, the tropical storm watch for Cat Island, Exuma, Long Island, Rum Cay, and San Salvador was upgraded to a tropical storm warning.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-50">\n        <a href="#cite_note-50">\n         [50]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       At 1515\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa026, the Bermuda Weather Service issued a tropical storm watch for Bermuda, reflecting the enormous size of the storm and the anticipated wide-reaching impacts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-51">\n        <a href="#cite_note-51">\n         [51]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States">\n        United States\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:White_House_teleconference_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2672" data-file-width="4008" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/White_House_teleconference_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/220px-White_House_teleconference_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/White_House_teleconference_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/330px-White_House_teleconference_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0c/White_House_teleconference_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/440px-White_House_teleconference_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:White_House_teleconference_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">\n          White House\n         </a>\n         conference with\n         <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">\n          FEMA\n         </a>\n         and\n         <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Homeland_Security" title="United States Department of Homeland Security">\n          Department of Homeland Security\n         </a>\n         in preparation for arrival of the hurricane.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <table class="mbox-small plainlinks sistersitebox" role="presentation" style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="415" data-file-width="759" height="22" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Wikinews-logo.svg/40px-Wikinews-logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Wikinews-logo.svg/60px-Wikinews-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/24/Wikinews-logo.svg/80px-Wikinews-logo.svg.png 2x" width="40"/>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text plainlist">\n         Wikinews has related news:\n         <i>\n          <b>\n           <a class="extiw" href="https://en.wikinews.org/wiki/U.S._prepares_for_arrival_of_Hurricane_Sandy" title="wikinews:U.S. prepares for arrival of Hurricane Sandy">\n            U.S. prepares for arrival of Hurricane Sandy\n           </a>\n          </b>\n         </i>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Much of the East Coast of the United States, in Mid-Atlantic and New England regions, had a good chance of receiving\n       <a href="/wiki/Gale" title="Gale">\n        gale\n       </a>\n       -force winds, flooding, heavy rain and possibly snow early in the week of October\xc2\xa028 from an unusual hybrid of Hurricane Sandy and a winter storm producing a\n       <a href="/wiki/Fujiwhara_effect" title="Fujiwhara effect">\n        Fujiwhara effect\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-52">\n        <a href="#cite_note-52">\n         [52]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Government weather forecasters said there was a 90% chance that the East Coast would be impacted by the storm. Jim Cisco of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hydrometeorological_Prediction_Center" title="Hydrometeorological Prediction Center">\n        Hydrometeorological Prediction Center\n       </a>\n       coined the term "Frankenstorm", as Sandy was expected to merge with a storm front a few days before Halloween.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-53">\n        <a href="#cite_note-53">\n         [53]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-54">\n        <a href="#cite_note-54">\n         [54]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-55">\n        <a href="#cite_note-55">\n         [55]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As coverage continued, several media outlets began eschewing this term in favor of "superstorm".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-foxnewssuperstorm_56-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-foxnewssuperstorm-56">\n         [56]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nofrankenstorm_57-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nofrankenstorm-57">\n         [57]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Utilities and governments along the East Coast attempted to head off long-term power failures Sandy might cause. Power companies from the Southeast to New England alerted\n       <a href="/wiki/Independent_contractor" title="Independent contractor">\n        independent contractors\n       </a>\n       to be ready to help repair storm damaged equipment quickly and asked employees to cancel vacations and work longer hours. Researchers from\n       <a href="/wiki/Johns_Hopkins_University" title="Johns Hopkins University">\n        Johns Hopkins University\n       </a>\n       , using a computer model built on power outage data from previous hurricanes, conservatively forecast that 10\xc2\xa0million customers along the Eastern Seaboard would lose power from the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-58">\n        <a href="#cite_note-58">\n         [58]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:President_Obama_discusses_preparations_for_Hurricane_Sandy.ogv" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         President Obama discusses preparations for Hurricane Sandy\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Through regional offices in\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlanta" title="Atlanta">\n        Atlanta\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">\n        Philadelphia\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">\n        New York City\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">\n        Boston\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">\n        Federal Emergency Management Agency\n       </a>\n       (FEMA) monitored Sandy, closely coordinating with state and tribal emergency management partners in Florida and the Southeast, Mid-Atlantic, and New England states.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">\n        <a href="#cite_note-59">\n         [59]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n        President Obama\n       </a>\n       signed emergency declarations on October 28 for several states expected to be impacted by Sandy, allowing them to request federal aid and make additional preparations in advance of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">\n        <a href="#cite_note-60">\n         [60]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flight cancellations and travel alerts on the U.S. East Coast were put in place in the Mid-Atlantic and the New England areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61">\n        <a href="#cite_note-61">\n         [61]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over 5,000 commercial airline flights scheduled for October 28 and October 29 were canceled by the afternoon of October\xc2\xa028\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">\n        <a href="#cite_note-62">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Amtrak" title="Amtrak">\n        Amtrak\n       </a>\n       canceled some services through October 29 in preparation for the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">\n        <a href="#cite_note-63">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition, the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._National_Guard" title="U.S. National Guard">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Air_Force" title="U.S. Air Force">\n        U.S. Air Force\n       </a>\n       put as many as 45,000\xc2\xa0personnel in at least seven states on alert for possible duty in response to the preparations and aftermath of Sandy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-64">\n        <a href="#cite_note-64">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Southeast">\n        Southeast\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sandy_Oct_28_2012_1600Z.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="9400" data-file-width="7200" height="287" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Sandy_Oct_28_2012_1600Z.jpg/220px-Sandy_Oct_28_2012_1600Z.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Sandy_Oct_28_2012_1600Z.jpg/330px-Sandy_Oct_28_2012_1600Z.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/29/Sandy_Oct_28_2012_1600Z.jpg/440px-Sandy_Oct_28_2012_1600Z.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sandy_Oct_28_2012_1600Z.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A tilted satellite image of the storm on October 28, with most of the U.S. coastline artificially highlighted. The entire east coast is visible, with a cloudless\n         <a href="/wiki/Florida" title="Florida">\n          Florida\n         </a>\n         coast seen at the bottom of the image and the outline of the coast of\n         <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">\n          Maine\n         </a>\n         at the top right.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Florida">\n        Florida\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Schools on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Treasure_Coast" title="Treasure Coast">\n        Treasure Coast\n       </a>\n       announced closures for October 26 in anticipation of Sandy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-65">\n        <a href="#cite_note-65">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A Russian\n       <a href="/wiki/Signals_intelligence_operational_platforms_by_nation#Russia:_Ship_Platforms" title="Signals intelligence operational platforms by nation">\n        intelligence-gathering ship\n       </a>\n       was allowed to stay in Jacksonville to avoid Sandy; the port is not far from\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kings_Bay_Naval_Submarine_Base" title="Kings Bay Naval Submarine Base">\n        Kings Bay Naval Submarine Base\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-66">\n        <a href="#cite_note-66">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Carolinas">\n        Carolinas\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       At 0900\xc2\xa0UTC on October\xc2\xa026, a tropical storm watch was issued from the mouth of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Savannah_River" title="Savannah River">\n        Savannah River\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Carolina" title="South Carolina">\n        South Carolina\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Oregon_Inlet" title="Oregon Inlet">\n        Oregon Inlet\n       </a>\n       , North Carolina, including\n       <a href="/wiki/Pamlico_Sound" title="Pamlico Sound">\n        Pamlico Sound\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-67">\n        <a href="#cite_note-67">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Twelve hours later, the portion of the tropical storm watch from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Santee_River" title="Santee River">\n        Santee River\n       </a>\n       in South Carolina to\n       <a href="/wiki/Duck,_North_Carolina" title="Duck, North Carolina">\n        Duck, North Carolina\n       </a>\n       , including Pamlico Sound, was upgraded to a warning.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-68">\n        <a href="#cite_note-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_North_Carolina" title="Governor of North Carolina">\n        Governor of North Carolina\n       </a>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Beverly_Perdue" title="Beverly Perdue">\n        Beverly Perdue\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency for\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_counties_in_North_Carolina" title="List of counties in North Carolina">\n        38\xc2\xa0eastern counties\n       </a>\n       on October\xc2\xa026, which took effect on the following day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-69">\n        <a href="#cite_note-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By October\xc2\xa029, the state of emergency was extended to 24\xc2\xa0counties in western North Carolina, with up to a foot (30 cm) of snow attributed to Sandy anticipated in higher elevations. The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Park_Service" title="National Park Service">\n        National Park Service\n       </a>\n       closed at least five sections of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Blue_Ridge_Parkway" title="Blue Ridge Parkway">\n        Blue Ridge Parkway\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-70">\n        <a href="#cite_note-70">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Virginia">\n        Virginia\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       On October\xc2\xa026,\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Virginia" title="Governor of Virginia">\n        Governor of Virginia\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Bob_McDonnell" title="Bob McDonnell">\n        Bob McDonnell\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency. The U.S. Navy sent more than twenty-seven ships and forces to sea from\n       <a href="/wiki/Naval_Station_Norfolk" title="Naval Station Norfolk">\n        Naval Station Norfolk\n       </a>\n       for their protection.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_71-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Governor McDonnell authorized the\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_National_Guard" title="Virginia National Guard">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       to activate 630 personnel ahead of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-72">\n        <a href="#cite_note-72">\n         [72]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Republican_Party_(United_States)" title="Republican Party (United States)">\n        Republican Party\n       </a>\n       presidential candidate\n       <a href="/wiki/Mitt_Romney" title="Mitt Romney">\n        Mitt Romney\n       </a>\n       canceled campaign appearances scheduled for October 28 in\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Beach,_Virginia" title="Virginia Beach, Virginia">\n        Virginia Beach, Virginia\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Hampshire" title="New Hampshire">\n        New Hampshire\n       </a>\n       October 30 because of Sandy. Vice President\n       <a href="/wiki/Joe_Biden" title="Joe Biden">\n        Joe Biden\n       </a>\n       canceled his appearance on October 27 in Virginia Beach and an October 29 campaign event in New Hampshire.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-73">\n        <a href="#cite_note-73">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       President Barack Obama canceled a campaign stop with former President\n       <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">\n        Bill Clinton\n       </a>\n       in Virginia scheduled for October 29, as well as a trip to\n       <a href="/wiki/Colorado_Springs,_Colorado" title="Colorado Springs, Colorado">\n        Colorado Springs, Colorado\n       </a>\n       , the next day because of the impending storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-74">\n        <a href="#cite_note-74">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mid-Atlantic">\n        Mid-Atlantic\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <h5>\n       <span id="Washington,_D.C.">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Washington.2C_D.C.">\n        Washington, D.C.\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       On October\xc2\xa026,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mayor_of_Washington,_D.C." title="Mayor of Washington, D.C.">\n        Mayor of Washington, D.C.\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Vincent_C._Gray" title="Vincent C. Gray">\n        Vincent Gray\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-75">\n        <a href="#cite_note-75">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which President Obama signed on October\xc2\xa028.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n        <a href="#cite_note-76">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Office_of_Personnel_Management" title="United States Office of Personnel Management">\n        United States Office of Personnel Management\n       </a>\n       announced federal offices in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington,_D.C." title="Washington, D.C.">\n        Washington, D.C.\n       </a>\n       area would be closed to the public on October 29\xe2\x80\x9330.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-77">\n        <a href="#cite_note-77">\n         [77]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition,\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington_Metropolitan_Area_Transit_Authority" title="Washington Metropolitan Area Transit Authority">\n        Washington D.C. Metro\n       </a>\n       service, both rail and bus, was canceled on October\xc2\xa029 due to expected high winds, the likelihood of widespread power outages, and the closing of the federal government.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-78">\n        <a href="#cite_note-78">\n         [78]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Smithsonian_Institution" title="Smithsonian Institution">\n        Smithsonian Institution\n       </a>\n       closed for the day of October\xc2\xa029.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bigstory.ap.org_79-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bigstory.ap.org-79">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Maryland">\n        Maryland\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_Maryland" title="Governor of Maryland">\n        Governor of Maryland\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Martin_O%27Malley" title="Martin O\'Malley">\n        Martin O\'Malley\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency on October\xc2\xa026.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_71-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By the following day,\n       <a href="/wiki/Smith_Island,_Maryland" title="Smith Island, Maryland">\n        Smith Island\n       </a>\n       residents were evacuated with the assistance of the Maryland Natural Resources Police,\n       <a href="/wiki/Dorchester_County,_Maryland" title="Dorchester County, Maryland">\n        Dorchester County\n       </a>\n       opened two shelters for those in flood prone areas, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_City,_Maryland" title="Ocean City, Maryland">\n        Ocean City\n       </a>\n       initiated Phase I of their Emergency Operations Plan.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-80">\n        <a href="#cite_note-80">\n         [80]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-81">\n        <a href="#cite_note-81">\n         [81]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-82">\n        <a href="#cite_note-82">\n         [82]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Baltimore Gas and Electric Co. put workers on standby and made plans to bring in crews from other states.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-The_Washington_Examiner_83-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-The_Washington_Examiner-83">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 28, President Obama declared an emergency in Maryland and signed an order authorizing the Federal Emergency Management Agency to aid in disaster relief efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-84">\n        <a href="#cite_note-84">\n         [84]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Also, numerous areas were ordered to be evacuated including part of\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_City,_Maryland" title="Ocean City, Maryland">\n        Ocean City\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Worcester_County,_Maryland" title="Worcester County, Maryland">\n        Worcester County\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Wicomico_County,_Maryland" title="Wicomico County, Maryland">\n        Wicomico County\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Somerset_County,_Maryland" title="Somerset County, Maryland">\n        Somerset County\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-85">\n        <a href="#cite_note-85">\n         [85]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-86">\n        <a href="#cite_note-86">\n         [86]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Officials warned that more than a hundred million tons of dirty sediment mixed with tree limbs and debris floating behind\n       <a href="/wiki/Conowingo_Dam" title="Conowingo Dam">\n        Conowingo Dam\n       </a>\n       could be eventually poured into the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n        Chesapeake Bay\n       </a>\n       , posing a potential environmental threat.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-87">\n        <a href="#cite_note-87">\n         [87]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Maryland_Transit_Administration" title="Maryland Transit Administration">\n        Maryland Transit Administration\n       </a>\n       canceled all service for October 29 and October 30. The cancellations applied to buses, light rail, and Amtrak and\n       <a href="/wiki/MARC_Train" title="MARC Train">\n        MARC\n       </a>\n       train service.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-88">\n        <a href="#cite_note-88">\n         [88]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 29, six shelters opened in\n       <a href="/wiki/Baltimore" title="Baltimore">\n        Baltimore\n       </a>\n       , and early voting was canceled for the day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bigstory.ap.org_79-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bigstory.ap.org-79">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Maryland Insurance Commissioner Therese M. Goldsmith activated an emergency regulation requiring pharmacies to refill prescriptions regardless of their last refill date.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-89">\n        <a href="#cite_note-89">\n         [89]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 29, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay_Bridge" title="Chesapeake Bay Bridge">\n        Chesapeake Bay Bridge\n       </a>\n       over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay" title="Chesapeake Bay">\n        Chesapeake Bay\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Millard_E._Tydings_Memorial_Bridge" title="Millard E. Tydings Memorial Bridge">\n        Millard E. Tydings Memorial Bridge\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Thomas_J._Hatem_Memorial_Bridge" title="Thomas J. Hatem Memorial Bridge">\n        Thomas J. Hatem Memorial Bridge\n       </a>\n       over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Susquehanna_River" title="Susquehanna River">\n        Susquehanna River\n       </a>\n       were closed to traffic in the midday hours.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-90">\n        <a href="#cite_note-90">\n         [90]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Delaware">\n        Delaware\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       On October 28, Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Jack_Markell" title="Jack Markell">\n        Markell\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency, with coastal areas of\n       <a href="/wiki/Sussex_County,_Delaware" title="Sussex County, Delaware">\n        Sussex County\n       </a>\n       evacuated.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wboc_91-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wboc-91">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In preparation for the storm, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Department_of_Transportation" title="Delaware Department of Transportation">\n        Delaware Department of Transportation\n       </a>\n       suspended some weekend construction projects, removed traffic cones and barrels from construction sites, and removed several span-wire overhead signs in Sussex County.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-92">\n        <a href="#cite_note-92">\n         [92]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Route_1" title="Delaware Route 1">\n        Delaware Route 1\n       </a>\n       through\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Seashore_State_Park" title="Delaware Seashore State Park">\n        Delaware Seashore State Park\n       </a>\n       was closed due to flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wboc_91-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wboc-91">\n         [91]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Delaware roads were closed to the public, except for emergency and essential personnel,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-93">\n        <a href="#cite_note-93">\n         [93]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and tolls on\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_95" title="Interstate 95">\n        I-95\n       </a>\n       and Delaware Route 1 were waived.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-94">\n        <a href="#cite_note-94">\n         [94]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/DART_First_State" title="DART First State">\n        DART First State\n       </a>\n       transit service was also suspended during the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-95">\n        <a href="#cite_note-95">\n         [95]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NJ_National_Guard_Prepares_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3744" data-file-width="5616" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/NJ_National_Guard_Prepares_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/220px-NJ_National_Guard_Prepares_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/NJ_National_Guard_Prepares_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/330px-NJ_National_Guard_Prepares_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/NJ_National_Guard_Prepares_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/440px-NJ_National_Guard_Prepares_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:NJ_National_Guard_Prepares_for_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Airmen of the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Jersey_National_Guard" title="New Jersey National Guard">\n          New Jersey National Guard\n         </a>\n         \'s 108th Wing assemble before being sent to assist at various emergency shelters.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:HurricaneSANDYCheltenham.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="996" data-file-width="1328" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/HurricaneSANDYCheltenham.jpg/220px-HurricaneSANDYCheltenham.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/HurricaneSANDYCheltenham.jpg/330px-HurricaneSANDYCheltenham.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/2d/HurricaneSANDYCheltenham.jpg/440px-HurricaneSANDYCheltenham.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:HurricaneSANDYCheltenham.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         A downed tree in\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cheltenham_Township,_Pennsylvania" title="Cheltenham Township, Pennsylvania">\n          Cheltenham Township, Pennsylvania\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Preparations began on October\xc2\xa026, when officials in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_May_County,_New_Jersey" title="Cape May County, New Jersey">\n        Cape May County\n       </a>\n       advised residents on\n       <a href="/wiki/Barrier_island" title="Barrier island">\n        barrier islands\n       </a>\n       to evacuate. There was also a voluntary evacuation for\n       <a href="/wiki/Mantoloking,_New_Jersey" title="Mantoloking, New Jersey">\n        Mantoloking\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Bay_Head,_New_Jersey" title="Bay Head, New Jersey">\n        Bay Head\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Barnegat_Light,_New_Jersey" title="Barnegat Light, New Jersey">\n        Barnegat Light\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Beach_Haven,_New_Jersey" title="Beach Haven, New Jersey">\n        Beach Haven\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Harvey_Cedars,_New_Jersey" title="Harvey Cedars, New Jersey">\n        Harvey Cedars\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Beach_Township,_New_Jersey" title="Long Beach Township, New Jersey">\n        Long Beach\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Ship_Bottom,_New_Jersey" title="Ship Bottom, New Jersey">\n        Ship Bottom\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Stafford_Township,_New_Jersey" title="Stafford Township, New Jersey">\n        Stafford\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_County,_New_Jersey" title="Ocean County, New Jersey">\n        Ocean County\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Ocean_County_96-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Ocean_County-96">\n         [96]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-97">\n        <a href="#cite_note-97">\n         [97]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bay_Head_98-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Bay_Head-98">\n         [98]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_New_Jersey" title="Governor of New Jersey">\n        Governor of New Jersey\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Chris_Christie" title="Chris Christie">\n        Chris Christie\n       </a>\n       ordered all residents of barrier islands from\n       <a href="/wiki/Sandy_Hook" title="Sandy Hook">\n        Sandy Hook\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_May,_New_Jersey" title="Cape May, New Jersey">\n        Cape May\n       </a>\n       to evacuate and closed\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_City,_New_Jersey" title="Atlantic City, New Jersey">\n        Atlantic City\n       </a>\n       casinos. Tolls were suspended on the northbound\n       <a href="/wiki/Garden_State_Parkway" title="Garden State Parkway">\n        Garden State Parkway\n       </a>\n       and the westbound\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_City_Expressway" title="Atlantic City Expressway">\n        Atlantic City Expressway\n       </a>\n       starting at 6 a.m. on October 28.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-99">\n        <a href="#cite_note-99">\n         [99]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       President Obama signed an emergency declaration for New Jersey, allowing the state to request federal funding and other assistance for actions taken before Sandy\'s landfall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-100">\n        <a href="#cite_note-100">\n         [100]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October\xc2\xa028,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mayor_of_Hoboken,_New_Jersey" title="Mayor of Hoboken, New Jersey">\n        Mayor of Hoboken\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Dawn_Zimmer" title="Dawn Zimmer">\n        Dawn Zimmer\n       </a>\n       ordered residents of basement and street-level residential units to evacuate, due to possible flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-101">\n        <a href="#cite_note-101">\n         [101]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 29, residents of\n       <a href="/wiki/Logan_Township,_New_Jersey" title="Logan Township, New Jersey">\n        Logan Township\n       </a>\n       were ordered to evacuate.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-102">\n        <a href="#cite_note-102">\n         [102]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Jersey_Central_Power_%26_Light" title="Jersey Central Power &amp; Light">\n        Jersey Central Power &amp; Light\n       </a>\n       told employees to prepare to work extended shifts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-The_Washington_Examiner_83-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-The_Washington_Examiner-83">\n         [83]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most schools, colleges and universities were closed October\xc2\xa029 while at least 509\xc2\xa0out of 580\xc2\xa0school districts were closed October\xc2\xa030.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NewsWorks_103-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NewsWorks-103">\n         [103]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Although tropical storm conditions were inevitable and hurricane-force winds were likely, the National Hurricane Center did not issue any tropical cyclone watches or warnings for New Jersey, because Sandy was forecast to become extratropical before landfall and thus would not be a tropical cyclone.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-104">\n        <a href="#cite_note-104">\n         [104]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Preparations in Pennsylvania began when\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_Pennsylvania" title="Governor of Pennsylvania">\n        Governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Tom_Corbett" title="Tom Corbett">\n        Tom Corbett\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency on October\xc2\xa026.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_71-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mayor_of_Philadelphia" title="Mayor of Philadelphia">\n        Mayor of Philadelphia\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Nutter" title="Michael Nutter">\n        Michael Nutter\n       </a>\n       asked residents in low-lying areas and neighborhoods prone to flooding to leave their homes by 1800\xc2\xa0UTC October\xc2\xa028 and move to safer ground.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-105">\n        <a href="#cite_note-105">\n         [105]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Philadelphia International Airport suspended all flight operations for October 29.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-106">\n        <a href="#cite_note-106">\n         [106]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October\xc2\xa029, Philadelphia shut down its mass transit system.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bigstory.ap.org_79-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bigstory.ap.org-79">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October\xc2\xa028,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/List_of_mayors_of_Harrisburg" title="List of mayors of Harrisburg">\n        Mayor of Harrisburg\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Linda_D._Thompson" title="Linda D. Thompson">\n        Linda D. Thompson\n       </a>\n       declared a state of disaster emergency for the city to go into effect at 5 a.m. October\xc2\xa029. Electric utilities in the state brought in crews and equipment from other states such as\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Mexico" title="New Mexico">\n        New Mexico\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Texas" title="Texas">\n        Texas\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Oklahoma" title="Oklahoma">\n        Oklahoma\n       </a>\n       , to assist with restoration efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-107">\n        <a href="#cite_note-107">\n         [107]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_York">\n        New York\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" during the storm.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image"
