</a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Governor_of_New_York" title="Governor of New York">\n        Governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Cuomo" title="Andrew Cuomo">\n        Andrew Cuomo\n       </a>\n       declared a statewide state of emergency and asked for a pre-disaster declaration on October\xc2\xa026,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-The_Wall_St._Journal_108-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-The_Wall_St._Journal-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which President Obama signed later that day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-109">\n        <a href="#cite_note-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By October\xc2\xa027, major carriers canceled all flights into and out of\n       <a href="/wiki/John_F._Kennedy_International_Airport" title="John F. Kennedy International Airport">\n        JFK\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/LaGuardia_Airport" title="LaGuardia Airport">\n        LaGuardia\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Newark_Liberty_International_Airport" title="Newark Liberty International Airport">\n        Newark-Liberty\n       </a>\n       airports, and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Metro-North_Railroad" title="Metro-North Railroad">\n        Metro North\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Long_Island_Rail_Road" title="Long Island Rail Road">\n        Long Island Rail Roads\n       </a>\n       suspended service.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MyFoxNY_110-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MyFoxNY-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Tappan_Zee_Bridge" title="Tappan Zee Bridge">\n        Tappan Zee Bridge\n       </a>\n       was closed,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-111">\n        <a href="#cite_note-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and later the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brooklyn_Battery_Tunnel" title="Brooklyn Battery Tunnel">\n        Brooklyn Battery Tunnel\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Holland_Tunnel" title="Holland Tunnel">\n        Holland Tunnel\n       </a>\n       were also closed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-112">\n        <a href="#cite_note-112">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On Long Island, an evacuation was ordered for\n       <a href="/wiki/South_Shore_(Long_Island)" title="South Shore (Long Island)">\n        South Shore\n       </a>\n       , including areas south of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sunrise_Highway" title="Sunrise Highway">\n        Sunrise Highway\n       </a>\n       , north of\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_State_Route_25A" title="New York State Route 25A">\n        Route 25A\n       </a>\n       , and in elevations of less than 16 feet (4.9\xc2\xa0m) above sea level on the\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Shore_(Long_Island)" title="North Shore (Long Island)">\n        North Shore\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-113">\n        <a href="#cite_note-113">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In\n       <a href="/wiki/Suffolk_County,_New_York" title="Suffolk County, New York">\n        Suffolk County\n       </a>\n       , mandatory evacuations were ordered for residents of\n       <a href="/wiki/Fire_Island" title="Fire Island">\n        Fire Island\n       </a>\n       and six towns.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-114">\n        <a href="#cite_note-114">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most schools closed in Nassau and Suffolk counties on October\xc2\xa029.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-115">\n        <a href="#cite_note-115">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hugh_L._Carey_Tunnel_during_Hurricane_Sandy_vc.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1118" data-file-width="1680" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Hugh_L._Carey_Tunnel_during_Hurricane_Sandy_vc.jpg/220px-Hugh_L._Carey_Tunnel_during_Hurricane_Sandy_vc.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Hugh_L._Carey_Tunnel_during_Hurricane_Sandy_vc.jpg/330px-Hugh_L._Carey_Tunnel_during_Hurricane_Sandy_vc.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/01/Hugh_L._Carey_Tunnel_during_Hurricane_Sandy_vc.jpg/440px-Hugh_L._Carey_Tunnel_during_Hurricane_Sandy_vc.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hugh_L._Carey_Tunnel_during_Hurricane_Sandy_vc.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The\n         <a href="/wiki/Brooklyn%E2%80%93Battery_Tunnel" title="Brooklyn\xe2\x80\x93Battery Tunnel">\n          Brooklyn\xe2\x80\x93Battery Tunnel\n         </a>\n         remained flooded on the Tuesday morning after the storm.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       New York City began taking precautions on October\xc2\xa026. Governor Cuomo ordered the closure of\n       <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Transportation_Authority" title="Metropolitan Transportation Authority">\n        MTA\n       </a>\n       and its subway on October\xc2\xa028, and the MTA suspended all subway, bus, and commuter rail service beginning at 2300\xc2\xa0UTC.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-116">\n        <a href="#cite_note-116">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Irene_in_New_York#New_York_City" title="Effects of Hurricane Irene in New York">\n        Hurricane Irene\n       </a>\n       nearly submerged subways and tunnels in 2011,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-117">\n        <a href="#cite_note-117">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       entrances and grates were covered just before Sandy, but were still flooded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-118">\n        <a href="#cite_note-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Port_Authority_Trans-Hudson" title="Port Authority Trans-Hudson">\n        PATH\n       </a>\n       train service and stations as well as the\n       <a href="/wiki/Port_Authority_Bus_Terminal" title="Port Authority Bus Terminal">\n        Port Authority Bus Terminal\n       </a>\n       were shut down in the early morning hours of October\xc2\xa029.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WABC_TV_119-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WABC_TV-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NY1_Transit_120-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NY1_Transit-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Later on October\xc2\xa028, officials activated the coastal emergency plan, with subway closings and the evacuation of residents in areas hit by\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irene" title="Hurricane Irene">\n        Hurricane Irene\n       </a>\n       in 2011. More than 76\xc2\xa0evacuation shelters were open around the city.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-The_Wall_St._Journal_108-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-The_Wall_St._Journal-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October\xc2\xa029, Mayor\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Bloomberg" title="Michael Bloomberg">\n        Michael Bloomberg\n       </a>\n       ordered public schools closed\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WABC_TV_119-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WABC_TV-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and called for a mandatory evacuation of Zone A, which comprised areas near coastlines or waterways.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-121">\n        <a href="#cite_note-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additionally, 200\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_York_National_Guard" title="New York National Guard">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       troops were deployed in the city.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NY1_Transit_120-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NY1_Transit-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/NYU_Langone_Medical_Center" title="NYU Langone Medical Center">\n        NYU Langone Medical Center\n       </a>\n       canceled all surgeries and medical procedures, except for emergency procedures.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NY1_Transit_120-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NY1_Transit-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Additionally, one of NYU Langone Medical Center\'s backup generators failed on October\xc2\xa029, prompting the evacuation of hundreds of patients, including those from the hospital\'s various\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Intensive_care_units" title="Intensive care units">\n        intensive care units\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-122">\n        <a href="#cite_note-122">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       U.S. stock trading was suspended for October 29\xe2\x80\x9330.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-123">\n        <a href="#cite_note-123">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_England">\n        New England\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Flooding_in_Marblehead_Massachusetts_caused_by_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2332" data-file-width="3484" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flooding_in_Marblehead_Massachusetts_caused_by_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/220px-Flooding_in_Marblehead_Massachusetts_caused_by_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flooding_in_Marblehead_Massachusetts_caused_by_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/330px-Flooding_in_Marblehead_Massachusetts_caused_by_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Flooding_in_Marblehead_Massachusetts_caused_by_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg/440px-Flooding_in_Marblehead_Massachusetts_caused_by_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Flooding_in_Marblehead_Massachusetts_caused_by_Hurricane_Sandy.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Flooding in\n         <a href="/wiki/Marblehead,_Massachusetts" title="Marblehead, Massachusetts">\n          Marblehead, Massachusetts\n         </a>\n         , caused by Hurricane Sandy on October 29.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Connecticut Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Dannel_Malloy" title="Dannel Malloy">\n        Dannel Malloy\n       </a>\n       partially activated the state\'s Emergency Operations Center on October 26\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CT.gov_124-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CT.gov-124">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and signed a Declaration of Emergency the next day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-governor.ct.gov_125-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-governor.ct.gov-125">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 28, President Obama approved Connecticut\'s request for an emergency declaration, and hundreds of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Connecticut_National_Guard" title="Connecticut National Guard">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       personnel were deployed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-thehour.com_126-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-thehour.com-126">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 29, Governor Malloy ordered road closures for all state highways.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">\n        <a href="#cite_note-127">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Numerous mandatory and partial evacuations were issued in cities across Connecticut.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ctnowevac_128-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ctnowevac-128">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Massachusetts Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Deval_Patrick" title="Deval Patrick">\n        Deval Patrick\n       </a>\n       ordered state offices to be closed October 29 and recommended schools and private businesses close. On October 28, President Obama issued a Pre-Landfall Emergency Declaration for Massachusetts. Several shelters were opened, and many schools were closed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-129">\n        <a href="#cite_note-129">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Massachusetts_Bay_Transportation_Authority" title="Massachusetts Bay Transportation Authority">\n        Massachusetts Bay Transportation Authority\n       </a>\n       shut down all services on the afternoon of October 29.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-130">\n        <a href="#cite_note-130">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 28, Vermont Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Peter_Shumlin" title="Peter Shumlin">\n        Peter Shumlin\n       </a>\n       , New Hampshire Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/John_Lynch_(New_Hampshire)" title="John Lynch (New Hampshire)">\n        John Lynch\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Maine" title="Maine">\n        Maine\n       </a>\n       \'s Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Paul_LePage" title="Paul LePage">\n        Paul LePage\n       </a>\n       all declared states of emergency.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bigstory.ap.org_79-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bigstory.ap.org-79">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131">\n        <a href="#cite_note-131">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-132">\n        <a href="#cite_note-132">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Appalachia_and_the_Midwest">\n        Appalachia and the Midwest\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       The National Weather Service issued a storm warning for\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Huron" title="Lake Huron">\n        Lake Huron\n       </a>\n       on October\xc2\xa029 that called for wave heights of 26 feet (7.9\xc2\xa0m), and possibly as high as 38 feet (12\xc2\xa0m).\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Michigan" title="Lake Michigan">\n        Lake Michigan\n       </a>\n       waves were expected to reach 19 feet (5.8\xc2\xa0m), with a potential of 33 feet (10\xc2\xa0m) on October\xc2\xa030.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Michigan_133-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Michigan-133">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Flood warnings were issued in\n       <a href="/wiki/Chicago" title="Chicago">\n        Chicago\n       </a>\n       on October\xc2\xa029, where wave heights were expected to reach 18 to 23 feet (5.5 to 7.0\xc2\xa0m) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Cook_County,_Illinois" title="Cook County, Illinois">\n        Cook County\n       </a>\n       and 25 feet (7.6\xc2\xa0m) in northwest\n       <a href="/wiki/Indiana" title="Indiana">\n        Indiana\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-134">\n        <a href="#cite_note-134">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Gale warnings were issued for Lake Michigan and\n       <a href="/wiki/Green_Bay_(Lake_Michigan)" title="Green Bay (Lake Michigan)">\n        Green Bay\n       </a>\n       in Wisconsin until the morning of October\xc2\xa031, and waves of 33 feet (10\xc2\xa0m) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Milwaukee" title="Milwaukee">\n        Milwaukee\n       </a>\n       and 20 feet (6.1\xc2\xa0m) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Sheboygan,_Wisconsin" title="Sheboygan, Wisconsin">\n        Sheboygan\n       </a>\n       were predicted for October\xc2\xa030.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GBPG_135-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-GBPG-135">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The actual waves reached about 20 feet (6.1\xc2\xa0m) but were less damaging than expected.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">\n        <a href="#cite_note-136">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-postcrescent_137-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-postcrescent-137">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The village of\n       <a href="/wiki/Pleasant_Prairie,_Wisconsin" title="Pleasant Prairie, Wisconsin">\n        Pleasant Prairie, Wisconsin\n       </a>\n       urged a voluntary evacuation of its lakefront area, though few residents signed up, and little flooding actually occurred.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-GBPG_135-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-GBPG-135">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-postcrescent_137-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-postcrescent-137">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Michigan" title="Michigan">\n        Michigan\n       </a>\n       was impacted by a winter storm system coming in from the west, mixing with cold air streams from the\n       <a href="/wiki/Arctic" title="Arctic">\n        Arctic\n       </a>\n       and colliding with Hurricane Sandy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Michigan_133-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Michigan-133">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The forecasts slowed shipping traffic on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Great_Lakes" title="Great Lakes">\n        Great Lakes\n       </a>\n       , as some vessels sought shelter away from the peak winds, except those on Lake Superior.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-138">\n        <a href="#cite_note-138">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-139">\n        <a href="#cite_note-139">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Detroit" title="Detroit">\n        Detroit\n       </a>\n       -based\n       <a href="/wiki/DTE_Energy" title="DTE Energy">\n        DTE Energy\n       </a>\n       released 100 contract line workers to assist utilities along the eastern U.S. with storm response, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Consumers_Energy" title="Consumers Energy">\n        Consumers Energy\n       </a>\n       did the same with more than a dozen employees and 120 contract employees.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wxyz_140-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wxyz-140">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Due to the widespread power outages, numerous schools had to close, especially in St. Clair County and areas along Lake Huron north of Metro Detroit.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-clickondetroit_141-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-clickondetroit-141">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As far as Ohio\'s western edge, areas were under a wind advisory.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-whiotvwind_142-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-whiotvwind-142">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All departing flights at\n       <a href="/wiki/Cleveland_Hopkins_International_Airport" title="Cleveland Hopkins International Airport">\n        Cleveland Hopkins International Airport\n       </a>\n       were canceled until October 30 at 3 p.m.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hopkins_flights_canceled_143-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hopkins_flights_canceled-143">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_West_Virginia" title="Governor of West Virginia">\n        Governor of West Virginia\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Earl_Ray_Tomblin" title="Earl Ray Tomblin">\n        Earl Ray Tomblin\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency ahead of storm on October\xc2\xa029.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-144">\n        <a href="#cite_note-144">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Up to 2 to 3\xc2\xa0feet (0.6\xe2\x80\x930.9\xc2\xa0m) of snow was forecast for mountainous areas of the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-washingtonpost1_145-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-washingtonpost1-145">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Canada">\n        Canada\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadian_Hurricane_Centre" title="Canadian Hurricane Centre">\n        Canadian Hurricane Centre\n       </a>\n       issued its first preliminary statement for Hurricane Sandy on October\xc2\xa025 from\n       <a href="/wiki/Southern_Ontario" title="Southern Ontario">\n        Southern Ontario\n       </a>\n       to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadian_Maritimes" title="Canadian Maritimes">\n        Canadian Maritimes\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-146">\n        <a href="#cite_note-146">\n         [146]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       with the potential for heavy rain and strong winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-147">\n        <a href="#cite_note-147">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October\xc2\xa029,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Environment_Canada" title="Environment Canada">\n        Environment Canada\n       </a>\n       issued severe wind warnings for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Great_Lakes" title="Great Lakes">\n        Great Lakes\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Lawrence_Valley" title="St. Lawrence Valley">\n        St. Lawrence Valley\n       </a>\n       corridor, from Southwestern Ontario as far as Quebec City.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-148">\n        <a href="#cite_note-148">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 30, Environment Canada issued storm surge warnings along the mouth of the St. Lawrence River.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-149">\n        <a href="#cite_note-149">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Rainfall warnings were issued for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Charlevoix" title="Charlevoix">\n        Charlevoix\n       </a>\n       region in Quebec, as well as for several counties in\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Brunswick" title="New Brunswick">\n        New Brunswick\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Nova_Scotia" title="Nova Scotia">\n        Nova Scotia\n       </a>\n       , where about 2 to 3 inches (51 to 76\xc2\xa0mm) of rain was to be expected.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-150">\n        <a href="#cite_note-150">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-151">\n        <a href="#cite_note-151">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">\n        <a href="#cite_note-152">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Freezing rain warnings were issued for parts of\n       <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ontario" title="Northern Ontario">\n        Northern Ontario\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-153">\n        <a href="#cite_note-153">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Impact">\n        Impact\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       At least 233 people were killed across the United States, the Caribbean, and Canada, as a result of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diakakis_et_al_2013_7-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Diakakis_et_al_2013-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-debris_154-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-debris-154">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WP_Deaths_155-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WP_Deaths-155">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Guardian_Deaths_156-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Guardian_Deaths-156">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-157">\n        <a href="#cite_note-157">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-usnews.nbcnews_158-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-usnews.nbcnews-158">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable sortable" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; border: <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Caribbean">\n        Caribbean\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Sandy_in_the_Greater_Antilles" title="Effects of Hurricane Sandy in the Greater Antilles">\n        Effects of Hurricane Sandy in the Greater Antilles\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Jamaica">\n        Jamaica\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       Jamaica was the first country directly affected by Sandy, which was also the first hurricane to make landfall on the island since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Gilbert" title="Hurricane Gilbert">\n        Hurricane Gilbert\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/1988_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="1988 Atlantic hurricane season">\n        24 years prior\n       </a>\n       . Trees and power lines were snapped and shanty houses were heavily damaged, both from the winds and flooding rains. More than 100 fishermen were stranded in outlying\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pedro_Cays" title="Pedro Cays">\n        Pedro Cays\n       </a>\n       off Jamaica\'s southern coast.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-170">\n        <a href="#cite_note-170">\n         [170]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Stones falling from a hillside crushed one man to death as he tried to get into his house in a rural village near Kingston.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-171">\n        <a href="#cite_note-171">\n         [171]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After 6 days another fatality recorded as a 27-year-old man, died due to electrocution, attempting a repair.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diakakis_et_al_2013_7-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Diakakis_et_al_2013-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The country\'s sole electricity provider, the Jamaica Public Service Company, reported that 70 percent of its customers were without power. More than 1,000 people went to shelters. Jamaican authorities closed the island\'s international airports, and police ordered 48-hour curfews in major towns to keep people off the streets and deter looting.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-172">\n        <a href="#cite_note-172">\n         [172]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most buildings in the eastern portion of the island lost their roofs.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated2_173-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated2-173">\n         [173]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage was assessed at approximately $100\xc2\xa0million throughout the country.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Hispaniola">\n        Hispaniola\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       In Haiti, which was still recovering from both the\n       <a href="/wiki/2010_Haiti_earthquake" title="2010 Haiti earthquake">\n        2010 earthquake\n       </a>\n       and the ongoing\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/2010%E2%80%932011_Haiti_cholera_outbreak" title="2010\xe2\x80\x932011 Haiti cholera outbreak">\n        cholera outbreak\n       </a>\n       , at least 54 people died,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WAVY_deaths_164-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WAVY_deaths-164">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and approximately 200,000 were left homeless as a result of four days of ongoing rain from Hurricane Sandy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-charles1_174-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-charles1-174">\n         [174]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Heavy damage occurred in\n       <a href="/wiki/Port-Salut" title="Port-Salut">\n        Port-Salut\n       </a>\n       after rivers overflowed their banks.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-175">\n        <a href="#cite_note-175">\n         [175]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the capital of\n       <a href="/wiki/Port-au-Prince" title="Port-au-Prince">\n        Port-au-Prince\n       </a>\n       , streets were flooded by the heavy rains, and it was reported that "the whole south of the country is underwater".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-176">\n        <a href="#cite_note-176">\n         [176]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most of the tents and buildings in the city\'s sprawling refugee camps and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cit%C3%A9_Soleil" title="Cit\xc3\xa9 Soleil">\n        Cit\xc3\xa9 Soleil\n       </a>\n       neighborhood were flooded or leaking, a repeat of what happened earlier in the year during the passage of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Isaac_(2012)" title="Hurricane Isaac (2012)">\n        Hurricane Isaac\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated2_173-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated2-173">\n         [173]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Crops were also wiped out by the storm and the country would be making an appeal for emergency aid.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-177">\n        <a href="#cite_note-177">\n         [177]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage in Haiti was estimated at $750 million (2012 USD), making it the costliest tropical cyclone in Haitian history.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SacBee_165-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SacBee-165">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the month following Sandy, a resurgence of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cholera" title="Cholera">\n        cholera\n       </a>\n       linked to the storm killed at least 44 people and infected more than 5,000 others.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HaitiCholera_167-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HaitiCholera-167">\n         [167]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In the neighboring\n       <a href="/wiki/Dominican_Republic" title="Dominican Republic">\n        Dominican Republic\n       </a>\n       , two people were killed and 30,000 people evacuated.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WP_Deaths_155-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WP_Deaths-155">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An employee of\n       <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">\n        CNN\n       </a>\n       estimated 70% of the streets in\n       <a href="/wiki/Santo_Domingo" title="Santo Domingo">\n        Santo Domingo\n       </a>\n       were flooded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-178">\n        <a href="#cite_note-178">\n         [178]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One person was killed in\n       <a href="/wiki/Juana_D%C3%ADaz,_Puerto_Rico" title="Juana D\xc3\xadaz, Puerto Rico">\n        Juana D\xc3\xadaz, Puerto Rico\n       </a>\n       after being swept away by a swollen river.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WP_Deaths_155-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WP_Deaths-155">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Cuba">\n        Cuba\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n     <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Michelle" title="Hurricane Michelle">\n          Michelle\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2001_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2001 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2001\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7009200000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $2\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cubdam_182-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-cubdam-182">\n           [182]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         <a class="mw-selflink selflink">\n          Sandy\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2012_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2012 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2012\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7009200000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $2\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-183">\n          <a href="#cite_note-183">\n           [183]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Dennis" title="Hurricane Dennis">\n          Dennis\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/2005_Atlantic_hurricane_season" title="2005 Atlantic hurricane season">\n          2005\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7009150000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $1.5\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CUBARAIN_184-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-CUBARAIN-184">\n           [184]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <th scope="row">\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Ivan" title="Hurricane Ivan">\n          Ivan\n         </a>\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a         7009120000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $1.2\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WMO_2004_185-0">\n          <a 2004\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <span class="sortkey" style="display:none">\n          7008923000000000000\xe2\x99\xa0\n         </span>\n         $923\xc2\xa0million\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WMO_2004_185-1">\n          <a href="#cite_note-WMO_2004-185">\n           [185]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Flickr_-_DVIDSHUB_-_Hurricane_Sandy_hits_Guantanamo_Bay_(Image_1_of_3).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="146" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Flickr_-_DVIDSHUB_-_Hurricane_Sandy_hits_Guantanamo_Bay_%28Image_1_of_3%29.jpg/220px-Flickr_-_DVIDSHUB_-_Hurricane_Sandy_hits_Guantanamo_Bay_%28Image_1_of_3%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Flickr_-_DVIDSHUB_-_Hurricane_Sandy_hits_Guantanamo_Bay_%28Image_1_of_3%29.jpg/330px-Flickr_-_DVIDSHUB_-_Hurricane_Sandy_hits_Guantanamo_Bay_%28Image_1_of_3%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/Flickr_-_DVIDSHUB_-_Hurricane_Sandy_hits_Guantanamo_Bay_%28Image_1_of_3%29.jpg/440px-Flickr_-_DVIDSHUB_-_Hurricane_Sandy_hits_Guantanamo_Bay_%28Image_1_of_3%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Flickr_-_DVIDSHUB_-_Hurricane_Sandy_hits_Guantanamo_Bay_(Image_1_of_3).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Hurricane Sandy damage in Guantanamo Bay\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       At least 55,000 people were evacuated before Hurricane Sandy\'s arrival.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-186">\n        <a href="#cite_note-186">\n         [186]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       While moving ashore, the storm produced waves up to 29 feet (9 meters) and a 6-foot (2 meter) storm surge that caused extensive coastal flooding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-187">\n        <a href="#cite_note-187">\n         [187]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There was widespread damage, particularly to Santiago de Cuba where 132,733 homes were damaged, of which 15,322 were destroyed and 43,426 lost their roof.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-CubaDamage_161-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-CubaDamage-161">\n         [161]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Electricity and water services were knocked out, and most of the trees in the city were damaged. Total losses throughout Santiago de Cuba province is estimated as high as $2 billion (2012 USD).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-HavanaTimes_162-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-HavanaTimes-162">\n         [162]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Sandy killed 11\xc2\xa0people in the country \xe2\x80\x93 nine in\n       <a href="/wiki/Santiago_de_Cuba_Province" title="Santiago de Cuba Province">\n        Santiago de Cuba Province\n       </a>\n       and two in\n       <a href="/wiki/Guant%C3%A1namo_Province" title="Guant\xc3\xa1namo Province">\n        Guant\xc3\xa1namo Province\n       </a>\n       ; most of the victims were trapped in destroyed houses.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-188">\n        <a href="#cite_note-188">\n         [188]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-189">\n        <a href="#cite_note-189">\n         [189]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This makes Sandy the deadliest hurricane to hit Cuba since 2005, when\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Dennis" title="Hurricane Dennis">\n        Hurricane Dennis\n       </a>\n       killed 16 people.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-190">\n        <a href="#cite_note-190">\n         [190]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Bahamas">\n        Bahamas\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       A\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Oceanic_and_Atmospheric_Administration" title="National Oceanic and Atmospheric Administration">\n        NOAA\n       </a>\n       automated station at\n       <a href="/wiki/West_End,_Grand_Bahama" title="West End, Grand Bahama">\n        Settlement Point\n       </a>\n       on\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Grand_Bahama_Island" title="Grand Bahama Island">\n        Grand Bahama Island\n       </a>\n       reported sustained winds of 49\xc2\xa0mph (74\xc2\xa0km/h) and a wind gust of 63\xc2\xa0mph (102\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-191">\n        <a href="#cite_note-191">\n         [191]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One person died from falling off his roof while attempting to fix a window shutter in the Lyford Cay area on New Providence. Another died in the Queen\'s Cove area on Grand Bahama Island where he drowned after the sea surge trapped him in his apartment.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WP_Deaths_155-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WP_Deaths-155">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Portions of the Bahamas lost power or cellular service, including an islandwide power outage on\n       <a href="/wiki/Bimini" title="Bimini">\n        Bimini\n       </a>\n       . Five homes were severely damaged near Williams\'s Town.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-192">\n        <a href="#cite_note-192">\n         [192]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Overall damage in the Bahamas was about $700 million (2012 USD), with the most severe damage on\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cat_Island_(Bahamas)" title="Cat Island (Bahamas)">\n        Cat Island\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Exuma" title="Exuma">\n        Exuma\n       </a>\n       where many houses were heavily damaged by wind and storm surge.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tribune242_169-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Tribune242-169">\n         [169]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Bermuda">\n        Bermuda\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Owing to the sheer size of the storm, Sandy also impacted Bermuda with high winds and heavy rains. On October\xc2\xa028, a weak\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Fujita_Scale" title="Fujita Scale">\n        F0\n       </a>\n       tornado touched down in\n       <a href="/wiki/Sandys_Parish" title="Sandys Parish">\n        Sandys Parish\n       </a>\n       , damaging homes and businesses.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-193">\n        <a href="#cite_note-193">\n         [193]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During a three-day span, the storm produced 0.98\xc2\xa0in (25\xc2\xa0mm) of rain at the\n       <a href="/wiki/L.F._Wade_International_Airport" title="L.F. Wade International Airport">\n        L.F. Wade International Airport\n       </a>\n       . The strongest winds were recorded on October\xc2\xa029: sustained winds reached 37\xc2\xa0mph (60\xc2\xa0km/h) and gusts peaked at 58\xc2\xa0mph (93\xc2\xa0km/h), which produced scattered minor damage.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-194">\n        <a href="#cite_note-194">\n         [194]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="United_States_2">\n        United States\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table align="right" border="1" class="wikitable" style=\'"margin:0\'>\n       <caption>\n        <a   <th>\n         9\n        </th>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Charley" title="Hurricane Charley">\n          Charley\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a
