$12\xc2\xa0billion\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr class="small">\n        <th colspan="6">\n         Source: National Hurricane Center\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Dead_2011_195-0">\n          <a href="#cite_note-Dead_2011-195">\n           [195]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-196">\n          <a href="#cite_note-196">\n           [196]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-197">\n          <a href="#cite_note-197">\n           [197]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-198">\n          <a href="#cite_note-198">\n           [nb 1]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Pier.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1366" data-file-width="2048" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Pier.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Pier.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Pier.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Pier.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Pier.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Pier.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Pier.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Damage to\n         <a href="/wiki/Casino_Pier" title="Casino Pier">\n          Casino Pier\n         </a>\n         in\n         <a href="/wiki/Seaside_Heights,_New_Jersey" title="Seaside Heights, New Jersey">\n          Seaside Heights\n         </a>\n         , New Jersey\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A total of 24\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._state" title="U.S. state">\n        U.S. states\n       </a>\n       were in some way affected by Sandy. The hurricane caused tens of billions of dollars in damage in the United States, destroyed thousands of homes, left millions without electric service,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-199">\n        <a href="#cite_note-199">\n         [198]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and caused 71 direct deaths in nine states, including 49 in New York, 10 in New Jersey, 3 in Connecticut, 2 each in Pennsylvania and Maryland, and 1 each in New Hampshire, Virginia and West Virginia.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diakakis_et_al_2013_7-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Diakakis_et_al_2013-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There were also 2 direct deaths from Sandy in U.S. coastal waters in the Atlantic Ocean, about 90 miles (150\xc2\xa0km) off the North Carolina coast, which are not counted in the U.S. total. In addition, the storm resulted in 87 indirect deaths.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In all, a total of 160 people were killed due to the storm, making Sandy the deadliest hurricane to hit the United States mainland since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Katrina" title="Hurricane Katrina">\n        Hurricane Katrina\n       </a>\n       in 2005 and the deadliest to hit the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States" title="East Coast of the United States">\n        U.S. East Coast\n       </a>\n       since\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Agnes" title="Hurricane Agnes">\n        Hurricane Agnes\n       </a>\n       in 1972.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-200">\n        <a href="#cite_note-200">\n         [199]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Due to flooding and other storm-related problems,\n       <a href="/wiki/Amtrak" title="Amtrak">\n        Amtrak\n       </a>\n       canceled all\n       <a href="/wiki/Acela_Express" title="Acela Express">\n        Acela Express\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Northeast_Regional" title="Northeast Regional">\n        Northeast Regional\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Keystone_Service" title="Keystone Service">\n        Keystone\n       </a>\n       , and Shuttle services for October 29 and 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-201">\n        <a href="#cite_note-201">\n         [200]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-202">\n        <a href="#cite_note-202">\n         [201]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       More than 13,000 flights were canceled across the U.S. on October 29, and more than 3,500 were called off October 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-msnbc_203-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-msnbc-203">\n         [202]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       From October 27 through early November 1, airlines canceled a total of 19,729 flights, according to\n       <a href="/wiki/FlightAware" title="FlightAware">\n        FlightAware\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-204">\n        <a href="#cite_note-204">\n         [203]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 31, over 6 million customers were still without power in 15 states and the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/District_of_Columbia" title="District of Columbia">\n        District of Columbia\n       </a>\n       . The states with the most customers without power were\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </a>\n       with 2,040,195 customers;\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_(state)" title="New York (state)">\n        New York\n       </a>\n       with 1,933,147;\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania" title="Pennsylvania">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </a>\n       with 852,458; and\n       <a href="/wiki/Connecticut" title="Connecticut">\n        Connecticut\n       </a>\n       with 486,927.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sandy_2012_rainfall.gif">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1364" data-file-width="723" height="321" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Sandy_2012_rainfall.gif/170px-Sandy_2012_rainfall.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Sandy_2012_rainfall.gif/255px-Sandy_2012_rainfall.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/45/Sandy_2012_rainfall.gif/340px-Sandy_2012_rainfall.gif 2x" width="170"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sandy_2012_rainfall.gif" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Storm total rainfall for Sandy (2012) across the United States\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_Stock_Exchange" title="New York Stock Exchange">\n        New York Stock Exchange\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nasdaq" title="Nasdaq">\n        Nasdaq\n       </a>\n       reopened on October 31 after a two-day closure for the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ABC_News_206-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ABC_News-206">\n         [205]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       More than 1,500 FEMA personnel were along the East Coast working to support disaster preparedness and response operations, including search and rescue, situational awareness, communications and logistical support. In addition, 28 teams containing 294 FEMA Corps members were pre-staged to support Sandy responders. Three federal urban search and rescue task forces were positioned in the Mid-Atlantic and ready to deploy as needed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ens-newswire_207-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ens-newswire-207">\n         [206]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On November 2, the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">\n        American Red Cross\n       </a>\n       announced they had 4,000 disaster workers across storm damaged areas, with thousands more\n       <i>\n        en route\n       </i>\n       from other states. Nearly 7,000 people spent the night in emergency shelters across the region.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-208">\n        <a href="#cite_note-208">\n         [207]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Sandy:_Coming_Together" title="Hurricane Sandy: Coming Together">\n         Hurricane Sandy: Coming Together\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , a live telethon on November 2 that featured rock and pop stars such as\n       <a href="/wiki/Bruce_Springsteen" title="Bruce Springsteen">\n        Bruce Springsteen\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Billy_Joel" title="Billy Joel">\n        Billy Joel\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Jon_Bon_Jovi" title="Jon Bon Jovi">\n        Jon Bon Jovi\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mary_J._Blige" title="Mary J. Blige">\n        Mary J. Blige\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Sting_(musician)" title="Sting (musician)">\n        Sting\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Christina_Aguilera" title="Christina Aguilera">\n        Christina Aguilera\n       </a>\n       , raised around $23 million for\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">\n        American Red Cross\n       </a>\n       hurricane relief efforts.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-209">\n        <a href="#cite_note-209">\n         [208]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As of November 5, 2012, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Hurricane_Center" title="National Hurricane Center">\n        National Hurricane Center\n       </a>\n       ranks Hurricane Sandy the second-costliest US hurricane since 1900 in constant 2010 dollars, and the sixth-costliest after adjusting for\n       <a href="/wiki/Inflation" title="Inflation">\n        inflation\n       </a>\n       , population and property values.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NHCStormCost_210-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NHCStormCost-210">\n         [209]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Their report also states that due to global warming the number of future hurricanes will "either decrease or remain essentially unchanged" overall, but the ones that do form will likely be stronger, with fiercer winds and heavier rains.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NHCStormCost_210-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NHCStormCost-210">\n         [209]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Scientists at the\n       <a href="/wiki/University_of_Utah" title="University of Utah">\n        University of Utah\n       </a>\n       reported the energy generated by Sandy was equivalent to "small earthquakes between magnitudes 2 and 3".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-211">\n        <a href="#cite_note-211">\n         [210]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Southeast_2">\n        Southeast\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Florida_2">\n        Florida\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       In South Florida, Sandy lashed the area with rough surf, strong winds, and brief squalls. Along the coast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Miami-Dade_County,_Florida" title="Miami-Dade County, Florida">\n        Miami-Dade County\n       </a>\n       , waves reached 10 feet (3.0\xc2\xa0m), but may have been as high as 20 feet (6.1\xc2\xa0m) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_County,_Florida" title="Palm Beach County, Florida">\n        Palm Beach County\n       </a>\n       . In the former county, minor pounding occurred on a few coastal roads. Further north in\n       <a href="/wiki/Broward_County,_Florida" title="Broward County, Florida">\n        Broward County\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida_State_Road_A1A" title="Florida State Road A1A">\n        State Road A1A\n       </a>\n       was inundated with sand and water, causing more than a 2 miles (3.2\xc2\xa0km) stretch of the road to be closed for the entire weekend. Additionally, coastal flooding extended inland up to 2\xc2\xa0blocks in some locations and a few houses in the area suffered water damage. In\n       <a href="/wiki/Manalapan,_Florida" title="Manalapan, Florida">\n        Manalapan\n       </a>\n       , which is located in southern Palm Beach County, several beachfront homes were threatened by erosion. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Worth,_Florida" title="Lake Worth, Florida">\n        Lake Worth\n       </a>\n       Pier was also damaged by rough seas. In Palm Beach County alone, losses reached $14\xc2\xa0million.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nwsmiami_212-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nwsmiami-212">\n         [211]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Sandy caused closures and cancellations of some activities at schools in\n       <a href="/wiki/Palm_Beach_County,_Florida" title="Palm Beach County, Florida">\n        Palm Beach\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Broward_County,_Florida" title="Broward County, Florida">\n        Broward\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Miami-Dade_County,_Florida" title="Miami-Dade County, Florida">\n        Miami-Dade\n       </a>\n       counties.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-213">\n        <a href="#cite_note-213">\n         [212]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Storm surge from Sandy also caused flooding and beach erosion along coastal areas in South Florida.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-214">\n        <a href="#cite_note-214">\n         [213]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Gusty winds also impacted South Florida, peaking at 67\xc2\xa0mph (108\xc2\xa0km/h) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Jupiter,_Florida" title="Jupiter, Florida">\n        Jupiter\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Fowey_Rocks_Light" title="Fowey Rocks Light">\n        Fowey Rocks Light\n       </a>\n       , which is near\n       <a href="/wiki/Key_Biscayne" title="Key Biscayne">\n        Key Biscayne\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nwsmiami_212-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-nwsmiami-212">\n         [211]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm left power outages across the region, which left many traffic lights out of order.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-215">\n        <a href="#cite_note-215">\n         [214]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In east-central Florida, damage was minor, though the storm left about 1,000 people without power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Orlando_216-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Orlando-216">\n         [215]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Airlines at\n       <a href="/wiki/Miami_International_Airport" title="Miami International Airport">\n        Miami International Airport\n       </a>\n       canceled more than 20 flights to or from\n       <a href="/wiki/Jamaica" title="Jamaica">\n        Jamaica\n       </a>\n       or\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Bahamas" title="The Bahamas">\n        the Bahamas\n       </a>\n       , while some airlines flying from\n       <a href="/wiki/Fort_Lauderdale%E2%80%93Hollywood_International_Airport" title="Fort Lauderdale\xe2\x80\x93Hollywood International Airport">\n        Fort Lauderdale\xe2\x80\x93Hollywood International Airport\n       </a>\n       canceled a total of 13 flights to the islands.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-autogenerated1_71-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-autogenerated1-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Coast_Guard" title="Coast Guard">\n        Coast Guard\n       </a>\n       rescued two sea men in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Volusia_County" title="Volusia County">\n        Volusia County\n       </a>\n       off\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Smyrna_Beach" title="New Smyrna Beach">\n        New Smyrna Beach\n       </a>\n       on the morning of October 26.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-217">\n        <a href="#cite_note-217">\n         [216]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Brevard_County" title="Brevard County">\n        Brevard\n       </a>\n       and Volusia Counties schools canceled all extracurricular activities for October 26, including football.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-218">\n        <a href="#cite_note-218">\n         [217]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Two\n       <a href="/wiki/Florida_panther" title="Florida panther">\n        panther\n       </a>\n       kittens escaped from the White Oak Conservation Center in Nassau County after the hurricane swept a tree into the fence of their enclosure; they were missing for 24 hours before being found in good health.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-219">\n        <a href="#cite_note-219">\n         [218]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="North_Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:121029-G-ZZ999-002_-_Coast_Guard_rescues_crewmembers_aboard_HMS.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="968" data-file-width="1296" height="164" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/121029-G-ZZ999-002_-_Coast_Guard_rescues_crewmembers_aboard_HMS.jpg/220px-121029-G-ZZ999-002_-_Coast_Guard_rescues_crewmembers_aboard_HMS.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/121029-G-ZZ999-002_-_Coast_Guard_rescues_crewmembers_aboard_HMS.jpg/330px-121029-G-ZZ999-002_-_Coast_Guard_rescues_crewmembers_aboard_HMS.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/2/27/121029-G-ZZ999-002_-_Coast_Guard_rescues_crewmembers_aboard_HMS.jpg/440px-121029-G-ZZ999-002_-_Coast_Guard_rescues_crewmembers_aboard_HMS.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:121029-G-ZZ999-002_-_Coast_Guard_rescues_crewmembers_aboard_HMS.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         The 180-foot (55 m) sailing ship,\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Bounty_(1960_ship)" title="Bounty (1960 ship)">\n           Bounty\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         , is shown nearly submerged during Hurricane Sandy in the Atlantic Ocean approximately 90 miles (140\xc2\xa0km) southeast of Hatteras, North Carolina on Monday, October 29, 2012.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On October 28, Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Bev_Perdue" title="Bev Perdue">\n        Bev Perdue\n       </a>\n       declared a state of emergency in 24 western counties, due to snow and strong winds.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-220">\n        <a href="#cite_note-220">\n         [219]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina" title="North Carolina">\n        North Carolina\n       </a>\n       was spared from major damage for the most part (except at the immediate coastline), though winds, rain, and mountain snow affected the state through October 30.\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocracoke,_North_Carolina" title="Ocracoke, North Carolina">\n        Ocracoke\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/North_Carolina_Highway_12" title="North Carolina Highway 12">\n        Highway 12\n       </a>\n       on\n       <a href="/wiki/Hatteras_Island" title="Hatteras Island">\n        Hatteras Island\n       </a>\n       were flooded with up to 2 feet (0.6\xc2\xa0m) of water, closing part of the highway, while 20 people on a fishing trip were stranded on\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Portsmouth_Island" title="Portsmouth Island">\n        Portsmouth Island\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-221">\n        <a href="#cite_note-221">\n         [220]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       There were three Hurricane Sandy-related deaths in the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diakakis_et_al_2013_7-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Diakakis_et_al_2013-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-222">\n        <a href="#cite_note-222">\n         [221]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On October 29, the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Coast_Guard" title="United States Coast Guard">\n        Coast Guard\n       </a>\n       responded to a distress call from\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Bounty_(1960_ship)" title="Bounty (1960 ship)">\n         Bounty\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , which was built for the 1962 movie\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Mutiny_on_the_Bounty_(1962_film)" title="Mutiny on the Bounty (1962 film)">\n         Mutiny on the Bounty\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       . It was taking on water about 90 miles (150\xc2\xa0km) southeast of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Hatteras" title="Cape Hatteras">\n        Cape Hatteras\n       </a>\n       . Sixteen people were on board.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-223">\n        <a href="#cite_note-223">\n         [222]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Coast Guard said the 16 people abandoned ship and got into two lifeboats, wearing survival suits and life jackets.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-224">\n        <a href="#cite_note-224">\n         [223]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The ship sank after the crew got off.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-225">\n        <a href="#cite_note-225">\n         [224]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Coast Guard rescued 14 crew members; another was found hours later but was unresponsive and later died.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bigstory_226-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bigstory-226">\n         [225]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The search for the captain, Robin Walbridge, was suspended on November 1, after efforts lasting more than 90 hours and covering approximately 12,000\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Square_nautical_miles" title="Square nautical miles">\n        square nautical miles\n       </a>\n       (41,100 km\xc2\xb2).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-washingtonpostbountysearchended_227-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-washingtonpostbountysearchended-227">\n         [226]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Virginia_2">\n        Virginia\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_hit_Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge_(VA)_(8141816490).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="768" data-file-width="1024" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Hurricane_Sandy_hit_Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28VA%29_%288141816490%29.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Sandy_hit_Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28VA%29_%288141816490%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Hurricane_Sandy_hit_Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28VA%29_%288141816490%29.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Sandy_hit_Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28VA%29_%288141816490%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cb/Hurricane_Sandy_hit_Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28VA%29_%288141816490%29.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Sandy_hit_Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28VA%29_%288141816490%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_hit_Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge_(VA)_(8141816490).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Damaged road at\n         <a href="/wiki/Chincoteague_National_Wildlife_Refuge" title="Chincoteague National Wildlife Refuge">\n          Chincoteague National Wildlife Refuge\n         </a>\n         on\n         <a href="/wiki/Assateague_Island" title="Assateague Island">\n          Assateague Island\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       On October 29, snow was falling in parts of the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-washingtonpost1_145-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-washingtonpost1-145">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Gov.\n       <a href="/wiki/Bob_McDonnell" title="Bob McDonnell">\n        Bob McDonnell\n       </a>\n       announced on October 30 that Virginia had been "spared a significant event", but cited concerns about rivers cresting and consequent flooding of major arteries. Virginia was awarded a federal disaster declaration, with Gov. McDonnell saying he was "delighted" that President Barack Obama and FEMA were on it immediately. At Sandy\'s peak, more than 180,000 customers were without power, most of whom were located in\n       <a href="/wiki/Northern_Virginia" title="Northern Virginia">\n        Northern Virginia\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-228">\n        <a href="#cite_note-228">\n         [227]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There were three Hurricane Sandy-related fatalities in the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diakakis_et_al_2013_7-10">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Diakakis_et_al_2013-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-usnews.nbcnews_158-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-usnews.nbcnews-158">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mid-Atlantic_2">\n        Mid-Atlantic\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <h5>\n       <span id="Maryland_and_Washington,_D.C.">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Maryland_and_Washington.2C_D.C.">\n        Maryland and Washington, D.C.\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Sandy_in_Maryland_and_Washington,_D.C." title="Effects of Hurricane Sandy in Maryland and Washington, D.C.">\n        Effects of Hurricane Sandy in Maryland and Washington, D.C.\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_flooding_Crisfield_MD.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="452" data-file-width="675" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Hurricane_Sandy_flooding_Crisfield_MD.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Sandy_flooding_Crisfield_MD.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Hurricane_Sandy_flooding_Crisfield_MD.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Sandy_flooding_Crisfield_MD.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/Hurricane_Sandy_flooding_Crisfield_MD.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Sandy_flooding_Crisfield_MD.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_flooding_Crisfield_MD.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Flooding in\n         <a href="/wiki/Crisfield,_Maryland" title="Crisfield, Maryland">\n          Crisfield, Maryland\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States" title="Supreme Court of the United States">\n        Supreme Court\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_Government" title="United States Government">\n        United States Government\n       </a>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Office_of_Personnel_Management" title="Office of Personnel Management">\n        Office of Personnel Management\n       </a>\n       were closed on October\xc2\xa030,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-229">\n        <a href="#cite_note-229">\n         [228]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-230">\n        <a href="#cite_note-230">\n         [229]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and schools were closed for two days.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-231">\n        <a href="#cite_note-231">\n         [230]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/MARC_train" title="MARC train">\n        MARC train\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Virginia_Railway_Express" title="Virginia Railway Express">\n        Virginia Railway Express\n       </a>\n       were closed on October 30, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Washington_Metropolitan_Area_Transit_Authority" title="Washington Metropolitan Area Transit Authority">\n        Metro\n       </a>\n       rail and bus service were on Sunday schedule, opening at 2 p.m., until the system closes.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wtop_232-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wtop-232">\n         [231]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       At least 100 feet (30 m) of a fishing pier in\n       <a href="/wiki/Ocean_City,_Maryland" title="Ocean City, Maryland">\n        Ocean City\n       </a>\n       was destroyed. Governor Martin O\'Malley said the pier was "half-gone".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-233">\n        <a href="#cite_note-233">\n         [232]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Due to high winds, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Chesapeake_Bay_Bridge" title="Chesapeake Bay Bridge">\n        Chesapeake Bay Bridge\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Millard_E._Tydings_Memorial_Bridge" title="Millard E. Tydings Memorial Bridge">\n        Millard E. Tydings Memorial Bridge\n       </a>\n       on\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/I-95" title="I-95">\n        I-95\n       </a>\n       were closed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-234">\n        <a href="#cite_note-234">\n         [233]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       During the storm, the Mayor of\n       <a href="/wiki/Salisbury,_Maryland" title="Salisbury, Maryland">\n        Salisbury\n       </a>\n       instituted a Civil Emergency and a curfew.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-235">\n        <a href="#cite_note-235">\n         [234]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_68" title="Interstate 68">\n        Interstate 68\n       </a>\n       in far western Maryland and northern\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">\n        West Virginia\n       </a>\n       closed due to heavy snow, stranding multiple vehicles and requiring assistance from the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Maryland_National_Guard" title="Maryland National Guard">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-236">\n        <a href="#cite_note-236">\n         [235]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Workers in\n       <a href="/wiki/Howard_County,_Maryland" title="Howard County, Maryland">\n        Howard County\n       </a>\n       tried to stop a sewage overflow caused by a power outage October 30. Raw sewage spilled at a rate of 2 million gallons per hour. It was unclear how much sewage had flowed into the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Little_Patuxent_River" title="Little Patuxent River">\n        Little Patuxent River\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-237">\n        <a href="#cite_note-237">\n         [236]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over 311,000 people were left without power as a result of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Delaware_2">\n        Delaware\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_impacts_Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge_(DE).jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="432" data-file-width="1143" height="83" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Hurricane_Sandy_impacts_Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28DE%29.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Sandy_impacts_Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28DE%29.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Hurricane_Sandy_impacts_Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28DE%29.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Sandy_impacts_Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28DE%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/cf/Hurricane_Sandy_impacts_Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28DE%29.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Sandy_impacts_Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge_%28DE%29.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_impacts_Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge_(DE).jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Before and after image of flooding caused by Hurricane Sandy at\n         <a href="/wiki/Prime_Hook_National_Wildlife_Refuge" title="Prime Hook National Wildlife Refuge">\n          Prime Hook National Wildlife Refuge\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       By the afternoon of October\xc2\xa029, rainfall at\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rehoboth_Beach" title="Rehoboth Beach">\n        Rehoboth Beach\n       </a>\n       totaled 6.53 inches (166\xc2\xa0mm). Other precipitation reports include nearly 7 inches (180\xc2\xa0mm) at\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Indian_River_Inlet" title="Indian River Inlet">\n        Indian River Inlet\n       </a>\n       and more than 4 inches (100\xc2\xa0mm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Dover,_Delaware" title="Dover, Delaware">\n        Dover\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Bear,_Delaware" title="Bear, Delaware">\n        Bear\n       </a>\n       . At 4\xc2\xa0p.m. on October\xc2\xa029,\n       <a href="/wiki/Delmarva_Power" title="Delmarva Power">\n        Delmarva Power\n       </a>\n       reported on its website that more than 13,900\xc2\xa0customers in Delaware and portions of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Shore_of_Maryland" title="Eastern Shore of Maryland">\n        Eastern Shore of Maryland\n       </a>\n       had lost electric service as high winds brought down trees and power lines. About 3,500\xc2\xa0of those were in\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Castle_County,_Delaware" title="New Castle County, Delaware">\n        New Castle County\n       </a>\n       , 2,900\xc2\xa0were in\n       <a href="/wiki/Sussex_County,_Delaware" title="Sussex County, Delaware">\n        Sussex\n       </a>\n       , and more than 100\xc2\xa0were in\n       <a href="/wiki/Kent_County,_Delaware" title="Kent County, Delaware">\n        Kent County\n       </a>\n       . Some residents in Kent and Sussex Counties experienced power outages that lasted up to nearly six\xc2\xa0hours. At the peak of the storm, more than 45,000 customers in Delaware were without power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-3">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Memorial_Bridge" title="Delaware Memorial Bridge">\n        Delaware Memorial Bridge\n       </a>\n       speed limit was reduced to 25\xc2\xa0mph (40\xc2\xa0km/h) and the two outer lanes in each direction were closed. Officials planned to close the span entirely if sustained winds exceeded 50\xc2\xa0mph (80\xc2\xa0km/h). A wind gust of 64\xc2\xa0mph (103\xc2\xa0km/h) was measured at\n       <a href="/wiki/Lewes,_Delaware" title="Lewes, Delaware">\n        Lewes\n       </a>\n       just before 2:30\xc2\xa0p.m. on October\xc2\xa029.\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_Route_1" title="Delaware Route 1">\n        Delaware Route 1\n       </a>\n       was closed due to water inundation between\n       <a href="/wiki/Dewey_Beach,_Delaware" title="Dewey Beach, Delaware">\n        Dewey Beach\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Fenwick_Island,_Delaware" title="Fenwick Island, Delaware">\n        Fenwick Island\n       </a>\n       . In Dewey Beach, flood waters were 1 to 2 feet (0.30 to 0.61\xc2\xa0m) in depth.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-238">\n        <a href="#cite_note-238">\n         [237]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Following the impact in Delaware, President Barack Obama declared the entire state a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_disaster_area" title="Federal disaster area">\n        federal disaster area\n       </a>\n       , providing money and agencies for disaster relief in the wake of Hurricane Sandy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-239">\n        <a href="#cite_note-239">\n         [238]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_Jersey_2">\n        New Jersey\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Sandy_in_New_Jersey" title="Effects of Hurricane Sandy in New Jersey">\n        Effects of Hurricane Sandy in New Jersey\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:121030-F-AL508-081c_Aerial_views_during_an_Army_search_and_rescue_mission_show_damage_from_Hurricane_Sandy_to_the_New_Jersey_coast,_Oct._30,_2012.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3523" data-file-width="5284" height="147" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/121030-F-AL508-081c_Aerial_views_during_an_Army_search_and_rescue_mission_show_damage_from_Hurricane_Sandy_to_the_New_Jersey_coast%2C_Oct._30%2C_2012.jpg/330px-121030-F-AL508-081c_Aerial_views_during_an_Army_search_and_rescue_mission_show_damage_from_Hurricane_Sandy_to_the_New_Jersey_coast%2C_Oct._30%2C_2012.jpg </a>\n         </div>\n         Damage to\n         <a href="/wiki/Mantoloking,_New_Jersey" title="Mantoloking, New Jersey">\n          Mantoloking, New Jersey\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       A 50-foot (15 m) piece of the Atlantic City Boardwalk washed away. Half the city of\n       <a href="/wiki/Hoboken,_New_Jersey" title="Hoboken, New Jersey">\n        Hoboken\n       </a>\n       flooded; the city of 50,000 had to evacuate two of its fire stations, the EMS headquarters, and the hospital. With the city cut off from area hospitals and fire suppression mutual aid, the city\'s Mayor asked for\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_Jersey_National_Guard" title="New Jersey National Guard">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       help.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bigstory_226-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bigstory-226">\n         [225]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the early morning of October 30, authorities in\n       <a href="/wiki/Bergen_County,_New_Jersey" title="Bergen County, New Jersey">\n        Bergen County\n       </a>\n       , New Jersey, evacuated residents after a\n       <a href="/wiki/Berm" title="Berm">\n        berm\n       </a>\n       overflowed and flooded several communities. Police Chief of Staff Jeanne Baratta said there were up to five feet (1.5 m) of water in the streets of\n       <a href="/wiki/Moonachie,_New_Jersey" title="Moonachie, New Jersey">\n        Moonachie\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Little_Ferry,_New_Jersey" title="Little Ferry, New Jersey">\n        Little Ferry\n       </a>\n       . The state Office of Emergency Management said rescues were undertaken in\n       <a href="/wiki/Carlstadt,_New_Jersey" title="Carlstadt, New Jersey">\n        Carlstadt\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-240">\n        <a href="#cite_note-240">\n         [239]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Baratta said the three towns had been "devastated" by the flood of water.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-241">\n        <a href="#cite_note-241">\n         [240]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At the peak of the storm, more than 2,600,000 customers were without power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There were 43 Hurricane Sandy-related deaths in the state of New Jersey.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Diakakis_et_al_2013_7-11">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Diakakis_et_al_2013-7">\n         [7]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-242">\n        <a href="#cite_note-242">\n         [241]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage in the state was estimated at $36.8 billion.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-243">\n        <a href="#cite_note-243">\n         [242]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Pennsylvania_2">\n        Pennsylvania\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_downed_tree_Kutztown_PA.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2304" data-file-width="3072" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Hurricane_Sandy_downed_tree_Kutztown_PA.jpg/220px-Hurricane_Sandy_downed_tree_Kutztown_PA.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Hurricane_Sandy_downed_tree_Kutztown_PA.jpg/330px-Hurricane_Sandy_downed_tree_Kutztown_PA.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ab/Hurricane_Sandy_downed_tree_Kutztown_PA.jpg/440px-Hurricane_Sandy_downed_tree_Kutztown_PA.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_downed_tree_Kutztown_PA.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Downed tree in\n         <a href="/wiki/Kutztown,_Pennsylvania" title="Kutztown, Pennsylvania">\n          Kutztown, Pennsylvania\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Philadelphia" title="Philadelphia">\n        Philadelphia\n       </a>\n       Mayor\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Nutter" title="Michael Nutter">\n        Michael Nutter\n       </a>\n       said the city would have no mass transit operations on any lines October 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ens-newswire_207-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ens-newswire-207">\n         [206]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       All major highways in and around the city of Philadelphia were closed on October 29 during the hurricane, including\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_95_in_Pennsylvania" title="Interstate 95 in Pennsylvania">\n        Interstate 95\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Blue_Route" title="Blue Route">\n        Blue Route\n       </a>\n       portion of\n       <a href="/wiki/Interstate_476" title="Interstate 476">\n        Interstate 476\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Vine_Street_Expressway" title="Vine Street Expressway">\n        Vine Street Expressway\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Schuylkill_Expressway" title="Schuylkill Expressway">\n        Schuylkill Expressway\n       </a>\n       (\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Interstate_76_(east)" title="Interstate 76 (east)">\n        I-76\n       </a>\n       ), and the Roosevelt Expressway;\n       <a href="/wiki/U.S._Route_1_in_Pennsylvania" title="U.S. Route 1 in Pennsylvania">\n        U.S. Route 1\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wpvi_244-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wpvi-244">\n         [243]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The highways reopened at 4 a.m. on October 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wpvi_244-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wpvi-244">\n         [243]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_River_Port_Authority" title="Delaware River Port Authority">\n        Delaware River Port Authority\n       </a>\n       also closed its major crossings over the\n       <a href="/wiki/Delaware_River" title="Delaware River">\n        Delaware River\n       </a>\n       between Pennsylvania and New Jersey due to high winds, including the\n       <a href="/wiki/Commodore_Barry_Bridge" title="Commodore Barry Bridge">\n        Commodore Barry Bridge\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/Walt_Whitman_Bridge" title="Walt Whitman Bridge">\n        Walt Whitman Bridge\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ben_Franklin_Bridge" title="Ben Franklin Bridge">\n        Ben Franklin Bridge\n       </a>\n       and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Betsy_Ross_Bridge" title="Betsy Ross Bridge">\n        Betsy Ross Bridge\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wpvi_244-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wpvi-244">\n         [243]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Trees and powerlines were downed throughout\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Altoona_Pennsylvania" title="Altoona Pennsylvania">\n        Altoona\n       </a>\n       , and four buildings partially collapsed.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-245">\n        <a href="#cite_note-245">\n         [244]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       More than 1.2 million were left without power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-bigstory.ap.org_79-4">\n        <a href="#cite_note-bigstory.ap.org-79">\n         [79]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Pennsylvania_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Pennsylvania Emergency Management Agency">\n        Pennsylvania Emergency Management Agency\n       </a>\n       reported 14 deaths believed to be related to Sandy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-246">\n        <a href="#cite_note-246">\n         [245]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_York_2">\n        New York\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Sandy_in_New_York" title="Effects of Hurricane Sandy in New York">\n        Effects of Hurricane Sandy in New York\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tmulti tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:308px;max-width:308px">\n        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:152px;max-width:152px">\n         <div class="thumbimage">\n          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NJ-NY_night_satellite_2012-08-31.jpg">\n           <img alt="" data-file-height="389" data-file-width="262" height="223" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/NJ-NY_night_satellite_2012-08-31.jpg/150px-NJ-NY_night_satellite_2012-08-31.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3e/NJ-NY_night_satellite_2012-08-31.jpg/225px-NJ-NY_night_satellite_2012-08-31.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3e/NJ-NY_night_satellite_2012-08-31.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n          </a>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n        <div class="tsingle" style="float:left;margin:1px;width:152px;max-width:152px">\n         <div class="thumbimage">\n          <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:NJ-NY_night_satellite_2012-11-01.jpg">\n           <img alt="" data-file-height="389" data-file-width="262" height="223"
