//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/8/8d/NJ-NY_night_satellite_2012-11-01.jpg 2x" width="150"/>\n          </a>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n        <div style="clear:left">\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption" style="clear:left;text-align:left;background-color:transparent">\n         <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">\n          NASA\n         </a>\n         satellite imagery showing the power outages in New York and New Jersey on November 1 compared to August 31.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_York_governor" title="New York governor">\n        New York governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Cuomo" title="Andrew Cuomo">\n        Andrew Cuomo\n       </a>\n       called\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/New_York_National_Guard" title="New York National Guard">\n        National Guard\n       </a>\n       members to help in the state. Storm impacts in\n       <a href="/wiki/Upstate_New_York" title="Upstate New York">\n        Upstate New York\n       </a>\n       were much more limited than in\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">\n        New York City\n       </a>\n       ; there was some flooding and a few downed trees.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-247">\n        <a href="#cite_note-247">\n         [246]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/Rochester,_New_York" title="Rochester, New York">\n        Rochester\n       </a>\n       area utilities reported slightly fewer than 19,000 customers without power, in seven counties.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-248">\n        <a href="#cite_note-248">\n         [247]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In the state as a whole, however, more than 2,000,000 customers were without power at the peak of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-5">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Mayor_of_New_York_City" title="Mayor of New York City">\n        Mayor of New York City\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Michael_Bloomberg" title="Michael Bloomberg">\n        Michael Bloomberg\n       </a>\n       announced that\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">\n        New York City\n       </a>\n       public schools would be closed on Tuesday, October 30 and Wednesday, October 31, but they remained closed through Friday, November 2.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-249">\n        <a href="#cite_note-249">\n         [248]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/CUNY" title="CUNY">\n        CUNY\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/NYU" title="NYU">\n        NYU\n       </a>\n       canceled all classes and campus activities for October 30.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-250">\n        <a href="#cite_note-250">\n         [249]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_Stock_Exchange" title="New York Stock Exchange">\n        New York Stock Exchange\n       </a>\n       was closed for trading for two days, the first weather closure of the exchange since 1985.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-251">\n        <a href="#cite_note-251">\n         [250]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It was also the first two-day weather closure since the Great\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Blizzard_of_1888" title="Blizzard of 1888">\n        Blizzard of 1888\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-252">\n        <a href="#cite_note-252">\n         [251]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The East River overflowed its banks, flooding large sections of\n       <a href="/wiki/Lower_Manhattan" title="Lower Manhattan">\n        Lower Manhattan\n       </a>\n       .\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Battery_Park" title="Battery Park">\n        Battery Park\n       </a>\n       had a water surge of 13.88\xc2\xa0ft.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-253">\n        <a href="#cite_note-253">\n         [252]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Seven subway tunnels under the\n       <a href="/wiki/East_River" title="East River">\n        East River\n       </a>\n       were flooded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-254">\n        <a href="#cite_note-254">\n         [253]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Transportation_Authority" title="Metropolitan Transportation Authority">\n        Metropolitan Transportation Authority\n       </a>\n       said that the destruction caused by the storm was the worst disaster in the 108-year history of the New York City subway system.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-255">\n        <a href="#cite_note-255">\n         [254]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Sea water flooded the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ground_Zero" title="Ground Zero">\n        Ground Zero\n       </a>\n       construction site.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-256">\n        <a href="#cite_note-256">\n         [255]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over 10 billion gallons of raw and partially treated sewage were released by the storm, 94% of which went into waters in and around New York and New Jersey.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-257">\n        <a href="#cite_note-257">\n         [256]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In addition, a four-story Chelsea building\'s facade crumbled and collapsed, leaving the interior on full display; however, no one was hurt by the falling masonry.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-258">\n        <a href="#cite_note-258">\n         [257]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Atlantic Ocean storm surge also caused considerable flood damage to homes, buildings, roadways, boardwalks and mass transit facilities in low-lying coastal areas of the outer boroughs of\n       <a href="/wiki/Queens" title="Queens">\n        Queens\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Brooklyn" title="Brooklyn">\n        Brooklyn\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Staten_Island" title="Staten Island">\n        Staten Island\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       After receiving many complaints that holding the marathon would divert needed resources, Mayor Bloomberg announced late afternoon November 2 that the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City_Marathon" title="New York City Marathon">\n        New York City Marathon\n       </a>\n       had been canceled. The event was to take place on Sunday, November 4. Marathon officials said that they did not plan to reschedule.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-259">\n        <a href="#cite_note-259">\n         [258]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Gas shortages throughout the region led to an effort by the U.S. federal government to bring in gasoline and set up mobile truck distribution at which people could receive up to 10 gallons of gas, free of charge. This caused lines of up to 20 blocks long and was quickly suspended.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-260">\n        <a href="#cite_note-260">\n         [259]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On Thursday, November 8, Mayor Bloomberg announced\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Odd-even_rationing" title="Odd-even rationing">\n        odd-even rationing\n       </a>\n       of gasoline would be in effect beginning November 9 until further notice.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-261">\n        <a href="#cite_note-261">\n         [260]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On November 26, Governor Cuomo called Sandy "more impactful" than Hurricane Katrina, and estimated costs to New York at $42 billion.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-262">\n        <a href="#cite_note-262">\n         [261]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Approximately 100,000 residences on Long Island were destroyed or severely damaged, including 2,000 that were rendered uninhabitable.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-263">\n        <a href="#cite_note-263">\n         [262]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There were 53 Hurricane Sandy-related deaths in the state of New York.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-264">\n        <a href="#cite_note-264">\n         [263]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       In 2016, the hurricane was determined to have been worst to strike the New York City area since at least 1700.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-265">\n        <a href="#cite_note-265">\n         [264]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="New_England_2">\n        New England\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Sandy_in_New_England" title="Effects of Hurricane Sandy in New England">\n        Effects of Hurricane Sandy in New England\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sandy_2012_snowfall.gif">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="933" data-file-width="1010" height="203" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Sandy_2012_snowfall.gif/220px-Sandy_2012_snowfall.gif" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Sandy_2012_snowfall.gif/330px-Sandy_2012_snowfall.gif 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/41/Sandy_2012_snowfall.gif/440px-Sandy_2012_snowfall.gif 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sandy_2012_snowfall.gif" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Sandy\'s storm total snowfall in inches across the Appalachians\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Wind gusts to 83\xc2\xa0mph were recorded on outer\n       <a href="/wiki/Cape_Cod" title="Cape Cod">\n        Cape Cod\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Buzzards_Bay" title="Buzzards Bay">\n        Buzzards Bay\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-266">\n        <a href="#cite_note-266">\n         [265]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Nearly 300,000 customers were without power in Massachusetts,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-6">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and roads and buildings were flooded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-267">\n        <a href="#cite_note-267">\n         [266]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Over 100,000 customers lost power in Rhode Island.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-268">\n        <a href="#cite_note-268">\n         [267]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Most of the damage was along the coastline, where some communities were flooded.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-269">\n        <a href="#cite_note-269">\n         [268]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Mount_Washington,_New_Hampshire" title="Mount Washington, New Hampshire">\n        Mount Washington\n       </a>\n       , New Hampshire saw the strongest measured wind gust from the storm at 140\xc2\xa0mph.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-270">\n        <a href="#cite_note-270">\n         [269]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Nearly 142,000 customers lost power in the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-7">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Appalachia_and_Midwest">\n        Appalachia and Midwest\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="West_Virginia">\n        West Virginia\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Sandy\'s rain became snow in the Appalachian mountains, leading to blizzard conditions in some areas, especially West Virginia,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-12">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       when a tongue of dense and heavy Arctic air pushed south through the region. This would normally cause a Nor\'easter, prompting some to dub Sandy a "nor\'eastercane" or "Frankenstorm".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-271">\n        <a href="#cite_note-271">\n         [270]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       There was 1\xe2\x80\x933 feet (30\xe2\x80\x9391\xc2\xa0cm) of snowfall in 28 of\n       <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">\n        West Virginia\n       </a>\n       \'s 55 counties.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-13">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-272">\n        <a href="#cite_note-272">\n         [271]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The highest snowfall accumulation was 36 inches (91\xc2\xa0cm) near\n       <a href="/wiki/Richwood,_West_Virginia" title="Richwood, West Virginia">\n        Richwood\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyTCR_3-14">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyTCR-3">\n         [3]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Other significant totals include 32 inches (81\xc2\xa0cm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Snowshoe,_West_Virginia" title="Snowshoe, West Virginia">\n        Snowshoe\n       </a>\n       , 29 inches (74\xc2\xa0cm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Quinwood,_West_Virginia" title="Quinwood, West Virginia">\n        Quinwood\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twcsandysnow_273-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twcsandysnow-273">\n         [272]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and 28 inches (71\xc2\xa0cm) in\n       <a href="/wiki/Davis,_West_Virginia" title="Davis, West Virginia">\n        Davis\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Flat_Top,_West_Virginia" title="Flat Top, West Virginia">\n        Flat Top\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Huttonsville,_West_Virginia" title="Huttonsville, West Virginia">\n        Huttonsville\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-274">\n        <a href="#cite_note-274">\n         [273]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       By the morning of October\xc2\xa031, there were still 36\xc2\xa0roads closed due to downed trees, powerlines, and snow in the road.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-twcsandysnow_273-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-twcsandysnow-273">\n         [272]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Approximately 271,800\xc2\xa0customers lost power during the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-8">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_pounds_West_Virginia.png">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1200" data-file-width="1600" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Hurricane_Sandy_pounds_West_Virginia.png/220px-Hurricane_Sandy_pounds_West_Virginia.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Hurricane_Sandy_pounds_West_Virginia.png/330px-Hurricane_Sandy_pounds_West_Virginia.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d7/Hurricane_Sandy_pounds_West_Virginia.png/440px-Hurricane_Sandy_pounds_West_Virginia.png 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hurricane_Sandy_pounds_West_Virginia.png" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Snow from Hurricane Sandy in\n         <a href="/wiki/West_Virginia" title="West Virginia">\n          West Virginia\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       There were reports of collapsed buildings in several counties due to the sheer weight of the wet, heavy snow.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-275">\n        <a href="#cite_note-275">\n         [274]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Overall, there were seven fatalities related to Hurricane Sandy and its remnants in West Virginia,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-276">\n        <a href="#cite_note-276">\n         [275]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       including John Rose, Sr., the Republican candidate for the state\'s 47th district in the state legislature, who was killed in the aftermath of the storm by a falling tree limb broken off by the heavy snowfall.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-277">\n        <a href="#cite_note-277">\n         [276]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Governor_of_West_Virginia" title="Governor of West Virginia">\n        Governor\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Earl_Ray_Tomblin" title="Earl Ray Tomblin">\n        Earl Ray Tomblin\n       </a>\n       asked President Obama for a federal disaster declaration, and on October\xc2\xa030, President Obama approved a state of emergency declaration for the state.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-278">\n        <a href="#cite_note-278">\n         [277]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Ohio">\n        Ohio\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       Wind gusts at\n       <a href="/wiki/Cleveland_Burke_Lakefront_Airport" title="Cleveland Burke Lakefront Airport">\n        Cleveland Burke Lakefront Airport\n       </a>\n       were reported at 68 miles per hour (109\xc2\xa0km/h).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rock_Hall_damaged_279-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Rock_Hall_damaged-279">\n         [278]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On October 30, hundreds of school districts canceled or delayed school across the state with at least 250,000\xc2\xa0homes and businesses without power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Schools_closed_Ohio.2C_snow_280-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Schools_closed_Ohio.2C_snow-280">\n         [279]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Damage was reported across the state including the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rock_and_Roll_Hall_of_Fame" title="Rock and Roll Hall of Fame">\n        Rock and Roll Hall of Fame\n       </a>\n       which lost parts of its siding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rock_Hall_damaged_279-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Rock_Hall_damaged-279">\n         [278]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Snow was reported in some parts of eastern\n       <a href="/wiki/Ohio" title="Ohio">\n        Ohio\n       </a>\n       and south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Cleveland" title="Cleveland">\n        Cleveland\n       </a>\n       . Snow and icy roads also were reported south of\n       <a href="/wiki/Columbus,_Ohio" title="Columbus, Ohio">\n        Columbus\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Schools_closed_Ohio.2C_snow_280-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Schools_closed_Ohio.2C_snow-280">\n         [279]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Michigan">\n        Michigan\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       The US Department of Energy reported that more than 120,000 customers lost power in Michigan as a result of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandySitRpt6_205-9">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandySitRpt6-205">\n         [204]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Weather_Service" title="National Weather Service">\n        National Weather Service\n       </a>\n       said that waves up to 23 feet (7 m) high were reported on southern Lake Huron.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-clickondetroit_141-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-clickondetroit-141">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h5>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Kentucky">\n        Kentucky\n       </span>\n      </h5>\n      <p>\n       More than one foot (300 mm) of snow fell in eastern Kentucky as Sandy merged with an\n       <a href="/wiki/Arctic_front" title="Arctic front">\n        Arctic front\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-281">\n        <a href="#cite_note-281">\n         [280]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Winter warnings in\n       <a href="/wiki/Harlan_County,_Kentucky" title="Harlan County, Kentucky">\n        Harlan\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Letcher_County,_Kentucky" title="Letcher County, Kentucky">\n        Letcher\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/Pike_County,_Kentucky" title="Pike County, Kentucky">\n        Pike County\n       </a>\n       were put into effect until October 31.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-282">\n        <a href="#cite_note-282">\n         [281]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Canada_2">\n        Canada\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Effects_of_Hurricane_Sandy_in_Canada" title="Effects of Hurricane Sandy in Canada">\n        Effects of Hurricane Sandy in Canada\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The remnants of Sandy produced high winds along\n       <a href="/wiki/Lake_Huron" title="Lake Huron">\n        Lake Huron\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Georgian_Bay" title="Georgian Bay">\n        Georgian Bay\n       </a>\n       , where gusts were measured at 105\xc2\xa0km/h (63\xc2\xa0mph). A 121\xc2\xa0km/h (72\xc2\xa0mph) gust was measured on top of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bluewater_Bridge" title="Bluewater Bridge">\n        Bluewater Bridge\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-283">\n        <a href="#cite_note-283">\n         [282]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One woman died after being hit by a piece of flying debris in\n       <a href="/wiki/Toronto" title="Toronto">\n        Toronto\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-debris_154-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-debris-154">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       At least 145,000 customers across Ontario lost power,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-284">\n        <a href="#cite_note-284">\n         [283]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and a Bluewater Power worker was electrocuted in Sarnia while working to restore power.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-285">\n        <a href="#cite_note-285">\n         [284]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Around 49,000 homes and businesses lost power in Quebec during the storm, with nearly 40,000 of those in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Laurentides" title="Laurentides">\n        Laurentides\n       </a>\n       region of the province, as well as more than 4,000 customers in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Townships" title="Eastern Townships">\n        Eastern Townships\n       </a>\n       and 1,700 customers in\n       <a href="/wiki/Montreal" title="Montreal">\n        Montreal\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-286">\n        <a href="#cite_note-286">\n         [285]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Hundreds of flights were canceled.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-287">\n        <a href="#cite_note-287">\n         [286]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Around 14,000 customers in\n       <a href="/wiki/Nova_Scotia" title="Nova Scotia">\n        Nova Scotia\n       </a>\n       lost power during the height of the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-288">\n        <a href="#cite_note-288">\n         [287]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Insurance Bureau of Canada\'s preliminary damage estimate was over $100 million for the nation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ca.finance.yahoo.com_160-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ca.finance.yahoo.com-160">\n         [160]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Aftermath">\n        Aftermath\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Relief_efforts">\n        Relief efforts\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RedCross_Obama_1.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1806" data-file-width="4078" height="97" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/RedCross_Obama_1.jpg/220px-RedCross_Obama_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/RedCross_Obama_1.jpg/330px-RedCross_Obama_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f2/RedCross_Obama_1.jpg/440px-RedCross_Obama_1.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:RedCross_Obama_1.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         October 30, 2012, President\n         <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n          Barack Obama\n         </a>\n         visits the\n         <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">\n          American Red Cross\n         </a>\n         Digital Command Center following Hurricane Sandy\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Several media organizations contributed to the immediate relief effort:\n       <a href="/wiki/Disney%E2%80%93ABC_Television_Group" title="Disney\xe2\x80\x93ABC Television Group">\n        Disney\xe2\x80\x93ABC Television Group\n       </a>\n       held a "Day of Giving" on Monday, November 5, raising $17 million on their television stations for the\n       <a href="/wiki/American_Red_Cross" title="American Red Cross">\n        American Red Cross\n       </a>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-ChicagoTri_289-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-ChicagoTri-289">\n         [288]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/NBC" title="NBC">\n        NBC\n       </a>\n       raised $23 million during their\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Sandy:_Coming_Together" title="Hurricane Sandy: Coming Together">\n         Hurricane Sandy: Coming Together\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       telethon the same day.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-RollingStone_290-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-RollingStone-290">\n         [289]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On 31 October 2012,\n       <a href="/wiki/News_Corporation" title="News Corporation">\n        News Corporation\n       </a>\n       donated $1 million to relief efforts in the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_metropolitan_area" title="New York metropolitan area">\n        New York metropolitan area\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-TheWrap_291-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-TheWrap-291">\n         [290]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of December 2013, the NGO\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Sandy_New_Jersey_Relief_Fund" title="Hurricane Sandy New Jersey Relief Fund">\n        Hurricane Sandy New Jersey Relief Fund\n       </a>\n       had distributed much of the funding raised in New Jersey.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Nahmias_292-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Nahmias-292">\n         [291]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On November 6, the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">\n        United Nations\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Food_Programme" title="World Food Programme">\n        World Food Programme\n       </a>\n       promised humanitarian aid to at least 500,000 people in\n       <a href="/wiki/Santiago_de_Cuba" title="Santiago de Cuba">\n        Santiago de Cuba\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-WashPost_293-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-WashPost-293">\n         [292]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On December 12, 2012, the\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/12-12-12:_The_Concert_for_Sandy_Relief" title="12-12-12: The Concert for Sandy Relief">\n         12-12-12: The Concert for Sandy Relief\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       took place at\n       <a href="/wiki/Madison_Square_Garden" title="Madison Square Garden">\n        Madison Square Garden\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/New_York_City" title="New York City">\n        New York City\n       </a>\n       . Various television channels in the United States and internationally aired the four-hour concert which was expected to reach over 1 billion people worldwide, featuring\n       <a href="/wiki/Bon_Jovi" title="Bon Jovi">\n        Bon Jovi\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Eric_Clapton" title="Eric Clapton">\n        Eric Clapton\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Dave_Grohl" title="Dave Grohl">\n        Dave Grohl\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Billy_Joel" title="Billy Joel">\n        Billy Joel\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Alicia_Keys" title="Alicia Keys">\n        Alicia Keys\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Chris_Martin" title="Chris Martin">\n        Chris Martin\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Paul_McCartney" title="Paul McCartney">\n        Paul McCartney\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Rolling_Stones" title="The Rolling Stones">\n        The Rolling Stones\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bruce_Springsteen_and_the_E_Street_Band" title="Bruce Springsteen and the E Street Band">\n        Bruce Springsteen and the E Street Band\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Roger_Waters" title="Roger Waters">\n        Roger Waters\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Eddie_Vedder" title="Eddie Vedder">\n        Eddie Vedder\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Kanye_West" title="Kanye West">\n        Kanye West\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/The_Who" title="The Who">\n        The Who\n       </a>\n       . Web sites including\n       <a href="/wiki/Fuse_(TV_channel)" title="Fuse (TV channel)">\n        Fuse.tv\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/MTV" title="MTV">\n        MTV.com\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/YouTube" title="YouTube">\n        YouTube\n       </a>\n       , and the sites of\n       <a href="/wiki/AOL" title="AOL">\n        AOL\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Yahoo!" title="Yahoo!">\n        Yahoo!\n       </a>\n       planned to\n       <a href="/wiki/Streaming_media" title="Streaming media">\n        stream\n       </a>\n       the performance.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-294">\n        <a href="#cite_note-294">\n         [293]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On December 28, 2012, the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">\n        United States Senate\n       </a>\n       approved an emergency\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Sandy_relief_bill" title="Hurricane Sandy relief bill">\n        Hurricane Sandy relief bill\n       </a>\n       to provide $60 billion for US states affected by Sandy,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-295">\n        <a href="#cite_note-295">\n         [294]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._House_of_Representatives" title="U.S. House of Representatives">\n        House\n       </a>\n       in effect postponed action until\n       <a href="/wiki/113th_United_States_Congress" title="113th United States Congress">\n        the next session\n       </a>\n       which began January 3 by adjourning without voting on the bill.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-296">\n        <a href="#cite_note-296">\n         [295]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On January 4, 2013 House leaders pledged to vote on a\n       <a href="/wiki/Flood_insurance" title="Flood insurance">\n        flood insurance\n       </a>\n       bill and an aid package by January 15.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-297">\n        <a href="#cite_note-297">\n         [296]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On January 28, the Senate passed the $50.5 billion Sandy aid bill by a count of 62\xe2\x80\x9336.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-298">\n        <a href="#cite_note-298">\n         [297]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       which President Obama signed into law January 29.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-299">\n        <a href="#cite_note-299">\n         [298]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In January 2013,\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_New_York_Times" title="The New York Times">\n         The New York Times\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       reported that those affected by the hurricane were still struggling to recover.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-300">\n        <a href="#cite_note-300">\n         [299]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In June 2013, NY Governor Andrew Cuomo set out to centralize recovery and rebuilding efforts in impacted areas of New York State by establishing the Governor\'s Office of Storm Recovery (GOSR). He aimed to address communities\' most urgent needs, and to identify innovative and enduring solutions to strengthen the State\'s infrastructure and critical systems. Operating under the umbrella of New York Rising, GOSR utilized approximately $3.8 billion in flexible funding made available by the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._Department_of_Housing_%26_Urban_Development" title="U.S. Department of Housing &amp; Urban Development">\n        U.S. Department of Housing &amp; Urban Development\n       </a>\n       \'s (HUD)\n       <a href="/wiki/Community_Development_Block_Grant" title="Community Development Block Grant">\n        Community Development Block Grant\n       </a>\n       Disaster Recovery (CDBG-DR) program to concentrate aid in four main areas: housing, small business, infrastructure, and the community reconstruction.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-301">\n        <a href="#cite_note-301">\n         [300]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On December 6, 2013, an analysis of\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">\n        Federal Emergency Management Agency\n       </a>\n       data showed that fewer than half of those affected who requested disaster recovery assistance had received any, and a total of 30,000 residents of New York and New Jersey remained displaced.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-302">\n        <a href="#cite_note-302">\n         [301]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In March 2014,\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Newsday" title="Newsday">\n         Newsday\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       reported, that 17 months after the hurricane people displaced from rental units on Long Island faced unique difficulties due to lack of affordable rental housing and delays in housing program implementations by New York State. Close to 9,000 rental units on Long Island were damaged by Hurricane Sandy in October 2012, and\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irene" title="Hurricane Irene">\n        Hurricane Irene\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Lee" title="Tropical Storm Lee">\n        Tropical Storm Lee\n       </a>\n       in 2011 per the NY State Governor\'s Office of Storm Recovery (GOSR).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-303">\n        <a href="#cite_note-303">\n         [302]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       New York State officials said that additional assistance would soon be available from the HUD\'s Community Development Block Grant funds via the New York Rising program.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-304">\n        <a href="#cite_note-304">\n         [303]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       On March 15, 2014, a group of those who remained displaced by the hurricane organized a protest at the Nassau Legislative building in Mineola, New York, to raise awareness of their frustration with the timeline for receiving financial assistance from the New York Rising program.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-305">\n        <a href="#cite_note-305">\n         [304]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       As of March 2014\n       <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">\n        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Sandy&amp;action=edit">\n         [update]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , the GOSR released a press statement, that the New York Rising Community Reconstruction Program had distributed more than $280 million in payments to 6,388 homeowners for damage from Hurricane Sandy,\n       <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Irene" title="Hurricane Irene">\n        Hurricane Irene\n       </a>\n       or\n       <a href="/wiki/Tropical_Storm_Lee" title="Tropical Storm Lee">\n        Tropical Storm Lee\n       </a>\n       . Every eligible homeowner who had applied by January 20, 2014 had been issued a check for home reconstruction, including over 4,650 Nassau residents for over $201 million and over 1,350 Suffolk residents for over $65 million. The State also had made offers over $293 million to buyout homes of 709 homeowners.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-306">\n        <a href="#cite_note-306">\n         [305]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Political_impact">\n        Political impact\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Political_impact_of_Hurricane_Sandy" title="Political impact of Hurricane Sandy">\n        Political impact of Hurricane Sandy\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" </a>\n         talking to storm victims in\n         <a href="/wiki/Brigantine,_New_Jersey" title="Brigantine, New Jersey">\n          Brigantine\n         </a>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n target="new" title="Play media">\n          <span class="play-btn-large">\n           <span class="mw-tmh-playtext">\n            Play media\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </div>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Chris_Christie_On_Post-Sandy_Obama_Meet-_%27I_Would_Do_It_Again%27_-_Morning_Joe_-_MSNBC.webm" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         \'Chris Christie On Post-Sandy Obama Meet- \'I Would Do It Again\n         <i>\n          video from\n          <a href="/wiki/MSNBC" title="MSNBC">\n           MSNBC\n          </a>\n          in 2017 in the aftermath of\n          <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Harvey" title="Hurricane Harvey">\n           Hurricane Harvey\n          </a>\n         </i>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Hurricane Sandy sparked much political commentary. Many scientists said warming oceans and greater atmospheric moisture were intensifying storms while rising sea levels were worsening coastal effects. November 2012 Representative\n       <a href="/wiki/Henry_Waxman" title="Henry Waxman">\n        Henry Waxman\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">\n        California\n       </a>\n       , the top Democrat of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/House_Energy_and_Commerce_Committee" title="House Energy and Commerce Committee">\n        House Energy and Commerce Committee\n       </a>\n       , requested a hearing in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lame_duck_session" title="Lame duck session">\n        lame duck session\n       </a>\n       on links between\n       <a href="/wiki/Climate_change" title="Climate change">\n        climate change\n       </a>\n       and Hurricane Sandy.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-307">\n        <a href="#cite_note-307">\n         [306]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Some news outlets labeled the storm the\n       <a href="/wiki/October_surprise" title="October surprise">\n        October surprise\n       </a>\n       of the\n       <a href="/wiki/United_States_presidential_election,_2012" title="United States presidential election, 2012">\n        2012 United States Presidential election\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-308">\n        <a href="#cite_note-308">\n         [307]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-309">\n        <a href="#cite_note-309">\n         [308]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       while Democrats and Republicans accused each other of\n       <a href="/wiki/Politicized_issue" title="Politicized issue">\n        politicizing\n       </a>\n       the storm.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-310">\n        <a href="#cite_note-310">\n         [309]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The storm hit the United States one week before its general\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/United_States_elections" title="United States elections">\n        United States elections\n       </a>\n       , and affected the presidential campaign, local and state campaigns in storm-damaged areas. New Jersey Governor\n       <a href="/wiki/Chris_Christie" title="Chris Christie">\n        Chris Christie\n       </a>\n       , one of\n       <a href="/wiki/Mitt_Romney" title="Mitt Romney">\n        Mitt Romney\n       </a>\n       \'s leading supporters, praised President\n       <a href="/wiki/Barack_Obama" title="Barack Obama">\n        Barack Obama\n       </a>\n       and his reaction to the hurricane, and toured storm-damaged areas of his state with the president.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-311">\n        <a href="#cite_note-311">\n         [310]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It was reported at the time that Sandy might affect elections in several states, especially by curtailing\n       <a href="/wiki/Early_voting" title="Early voting">\n        early voting\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-312">\n        <a href="#cite_note-312">\n         [311]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/The_Economist" title="The Economist">\n         The Economist\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       wrote, "[...]the weather is supposed to clear up well ahead of election day, but the impact could be felt in the turnout of early voters."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-313">\n        <a href="#cite_note-313">\n         [312]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <a href="/wiki/ABC_News" title="ABC News">\n        ABC News\n       </a>\n       predicted this might be offset by a tendency to clear roads and restore power more quickly in urban areas.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-314">\n        <a href="#cite_note-314">\n         [313]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The storm ignited a debate over whether Republican presidential nominee Mitt Romney in 2011 proposed to eliminate the\n       <a href="/wiki/Federal_Emergency_Management_Agency" title="Federal Emergency Management Agency">\n        Federal Emergency Management Agency\n       </a>\n       (FEMA).\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-315">\n        <a href="#cite_note-315">\n         [314]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The next day the Romney campaign promised to keep FEMA funded, but did not explain what other parts of the federal budget it would cut to pay for it.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-316">\n        <a href="#cite_note-316">\n         [315]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Beyond the election,\n       <i>\n        National Defense Magazine\n       </i>\n       said Sandy "might cause a rethinking (in the USA) of how climate change threatens national security".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-317">\n        <a href="#cite_note-317">\n         [316]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       In his news conference on November 14, President Obama said "... we can\'t attribute any particular weather event to climate change. What we do know is the temperature around the globe is increasing faster than was predicted even 10 years ago. We do know that the Arctic ice cap is melting faster than was predicted even five years ago. We do know that there have been extraordinarily \xe2\x80\x94 there have been an extraordinarily large number of severe weather events here in North America, but also around the globe. And I am a firm believer that climate change is real, that it is impacted by human behavior and carbon emissions. And as a consequence, I think we\'ve got an obligation to future generations to do something about it."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-318">\n        <a href="#cite_note-318">\n         [317]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On January 30, 2015, days after the U.S. Army Corps of Engineers released a post-Sandy report examining flood risks for 31,200 miles (50,210 km) of the North Atlantic coast, President Obama issued an executive order directing federal agencies, state and local governments drawing federal funds to adopt stricter building and siting standards to reflect scientific projections that future flooding will be more frequent and intense due to climate change.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-319">\n        <a href="#cite_note-319">\n         [318]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Financial_markets_impact">\n        Financial markets impact\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Update" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <div style="width:52px">\n          <img alt="Ambox current red.svg" data-file-height="290" data-file-width="360" height="34" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/42px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/63px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/98/Ambox_current_red.svg/84px-Ambox_current_red.svg.png 2x" width="42"/>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n         <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          This section needs to be\n          <b>\n           updated\n          </b>\n          .\n          <span class="hide-when-compact">\n           Please update this article to reflect recent events or newly available information.\n          </span>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (March 2017)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Power outages and flooding in the area closed the New York Stock Exchange and other financial markets on both October 29 and 30, a weather-related closure that last happened in 1888.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-320">\n        <a href="#cite_note-320">\n         [319]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       When markets reopened on October 31, investors were relieved that it closed relatively flat that day. A week later, the\n       <a href="/wiki/National_Association_of_Insurance_Commissioners" title="National Association of Insurance Commissioners">\n        National Association of Insurance Commissioners\n       </a>\n       Capital Markets Bureau noted a slight uptick in the market (0.8%) and suggested that the negative economic impact of Hurricane Sandy was offset by the expected positive impacts of rebuilding.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-321">\n        <a href="#cite_note-321">\n         [320]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Media_coverage">\n        Media coverage\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       As Hurricane Sandy approached the United States, forecasters and journalists gave it several different unofficial names, at first related to its projected snow content, then to its proximity to Halloween, and eventually to the overall size of the storm. Early nicknames included "Snowicane Sandy"\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-322">\n        <a href="#cite_note-322">\n         [321]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Nor%27easter" title="Nor\'easter">\n        "Snor\'eastercane\n       </a>\n       Sandy".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-323">\n        <a href="#cite_note-323">\n         [322]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-324">\n        <a href="#cite_note-324">\n         [323]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The most popular Halloween-related nickname was "Frankenstorm",\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-325">\n        <a href="#cite_note-325">\n         [324]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-326">\n        <a href="#cite_note-326">\n         [325]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       coined by Jim Cisco, a forecaster at the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Hydrometeorological_Prediction_Center" title="Hydrometeorological Prediction Center">\n        Hydrometeorological Prediction Center\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-327">\n        <a href="#cite_note-327">\n         [326]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-328">\n        <a href="#cite_note-328">\n         [327]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-329">\n        <a href="#cite_note-329">\n         [328]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       CNN banned the use of the term, saying it trivialized the destruction.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-330">\n        <a href="#cite_note-330">\n         [329]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-331">\n        <a href="#cite_note-331">\n         [330]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       The severe and widespread damage the storm caused in the United States, as well as its unusual merger with a frontal system, resulted in the nicknaming of the hurricane "Superstorm Sandy" by the media, public officials, and several organizations, including U.S. government agencies.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyDebris_332-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyDebris-332">\n         [331]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SandyUnusual_333-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SandyUnusual-333">\n         [332]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-BlameGame_334-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-BlameGame-334">\n         [333]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Supersturms_335-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Supersturms-335">\n         [334]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-336">\n        <a href="#cite_note-336">\n         [335]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-337">\n        <a href="#cite_note-337">\n         [336]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-338">\n        <a href="#cite_note-338">\n         [337]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This persisted as the most common nickname well into 2013.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-339">\n        <a href="#cite_note-339">\n         [338]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-340">\n        <a href="#cite_note-340">\n         [339]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The term was also embraced by climate change proponents as a term for the new type of storms caused by global warming,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-341">\n        <a href="#cite_note-341">\n         [340]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">\n        [\n        <i>\n         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:No_original_research#Synthesis_of_published_material" title="Wikipedia:No original research">\n          <span title="The material near this tag may be based upon an improper synthesis of sources. (September 2013)">\n           improper synthesis?\n          </span>\n         </a>\n        </i>\n        ]\n       </sup>\n       while other writers used the term but maintained that it was too soon to blame the storm on climate change.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-342">\n        <a href="#cite_note-342">\n         [341]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-343">\n        <a href="#cite_note-343">\n         [342]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Meanwhile,\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Popular_Science" title="Popular Science">\n         Popular Science\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       called it "an imaginary scare-term that exists exclusively for shock value".\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-344">\n        <a href="#cite_note-344">\n         [343]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Insurance_fraud_claims">\n        Insurance fraud claims\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Thousands of homeowners were denied their flood insurance claims based upon fraudulent engineers\' reports, according to the whistleblowing efforts of Andrew Braum, an engineer who claimed that at least 175 of his more than 180 inspections were doctored.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-345">\n        <a href="#cite_note-345">\n         [344]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-346">\n        <a href="#cite_note-346">\n         [345]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As a result, a class-action racketeering lawsuit has been filed against several insurance companies and their contract engineering firms.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-347">\n        <a href="#cite_note-347">\n         [346]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       As of 2015\n       <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">\n        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Hurricane_Sandy&amp;action=edit">\n         [update]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , the Federal Emergency Management Agency planned to review all flood insurance claims.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-348">\n        <a href="#cite_note-348">\n         [347]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Baby_boom">\n        Baby boom\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       New Jersey hospitals saw a spike in births nine months after Sandy, causing some to believe that there was a post-Sandy baby boom. The\n       <a href="/wiki/Monmouth_Medical_Center" title="Monmouth Medical Center">\n        Monmouth Medical Center\n       </a>\n       saw a 35% jump, and two other hospitals saw 20% increases.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-349">\n        <a href="#cite_note-349">\n         [348]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       An expert stated that post-storm births that year were higher than in past disasters.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-350">\n        <a href="#cite_note-350">\n         [349]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Retirement_of_the_name">\n        Retirement of the name\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_retired_Atlantic_hurricane_names" title="List of retired Atlantic hurricane names">\n        List of retired Atlantic hurricane names\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Because of the exceptional damage and deaths caused by the storm in many countries, the name\n       <i>\n        Sandy\n       </i>\n       was later retired by the\n       <a href="/wiki/World_Meteorological_Organization" title="World Meteorological Organization">\n        World Meteorological Organization\n       </a>\n       , and will never be used again for a\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/North_Atlantic_hurricane" title="North Atlantic hurricane">\n        North Atlantic hurricane\n       </a>\n       . The name was replaced with\n       <i>\n        Sara\n       </i>\n       for the 2018 Atlantic hurricane season.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-351">\n        <a href="#cite_note-351">\n         [350]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="In_popular_culture">\n        In popular culture\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       In the\n       <a href="/wiki/Syfy" title="Syfy">\n        Syfy\n       </a>\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Television_movie" title="Television movie">\n        television movie\n       </a>\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Sharknado_3:_Oh_Hell_No!" title="Sharknado 3: Oh Hell No!">\n         Sharknado 3: Oh Hell No!\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , a radar image of Sandy can be seen (close to its landfall in\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Jersey" title="New Jersey">\n        New Jersey\n       </a>\n       ), but represented fictionally as an unnamed tropical storm heading towards\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Washington_D.C" title="Washington D.C">\n        Washington D.C\n       </a>\n       . The storm is also featured in an episode of\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Shades_of_Blue_(TV_series)" title="Shades of Blue (TV series)">\n         Shades of Blue\n        </a>\n        .\n       </i>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <div aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Ajournal&amp;rft.genre=article&amp;rft.jtitle=The+New+York+Times%3B+Dot+Earth&amp;rft.atitle=The+%23Frankenstorm+in+Climate+Context&amp;rft.date=2012-10-28&amp;rft.aulast=Andrew+C.&amp;rft.aufirst=Revkin&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Fdotearth.blogs.nytimes.com%2F2012%2F10%2F28%2Fthe-frankenstorm-in-climate-context%2F&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AHurricane+Sandy">\n      ^\n          <a href="#cite_ref-SurfTemps_37-0">\n           <sup>\n            <i>\n             <b>\n              a\n             </b>\n            </i>\n           </sup>\n          </a>\n   <span class="reference-text">\n          <cite class="citation web">\n           Trenberth, Kevin.\n           <a class="external text" href="http://theconversation.edu.au/hurricane-sandy-mixes-super-storm-conditions-with-climate-change-10388" rel="nofollow">\n            "Hurricane Sandy mixes super-storm conditions with climate change"\n           </a>\n           . The Conversation\n           <span class="reference-accessdate">\n            . Retrieved\n            <span class="nowrap">\n             2012-10-29\n            </span>\n           </span>\n           .\n           <q>\n            The sea surface temperatures along the Atlantic coast have been running at over 3\n            <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%C2%B0C" title="\xc2\xb0C">\n             \xc2\xb0C\n            </a>\n            above normal for a region extending 800 km off shore all the way from Florida to Canada. Global warming contributes 0.6\xc2\xb0C to this. With every degree C, the water holding of the atmosphere goes up 7%, and the moisture provides fuel for the tropical storm, increases its intensity, and magnifies the rainfall by double that amount compared with normal conditions. Global climate change has contributed to the higher sea surface and ocean temperatures, and a warmer and moister atmosphere, and its effects are in the range of 5 to 10%. Natural variability and weather has provided the perhaps optimal conditions of a hurricane running into extra-tropical conditions to make for a huge intense storm, enhanced by global warming influences.\n           </q>\n          </cite>\n          <span class="Z3988" title="ctx_ver=Z39.88-2004&amp;rft_val_fmt=info%3Aofi%2Ffmt%3Akev%3Amtx%3Abook&amp;rft.genre=unknown&amp;rft.btitle=Hurricane+Sandy+mixes+super-storm+conditions+with+climate+change&amp;rft.pub=The+Conversation&amp;rft.aulast=Trenberth&amp;rft.aufirst=Kevin&amp;rft_id=http%3A%2F%2Ftheconversation.edu.au%2Fhurricane-sandy-mixes-super-storm-conditions-with-climate-change-10388&amp;rfr_id=info%3Asid%2Fen.wikipedia.org%3AHurricane+Sandy">\n           <span style="display:none;">\n           </span>\n          </span>\n         </span>\n        </li>\n        <li id="cite_note-Masters-38">\n         <span class="mw-cite-backlink">\n          ^\n          <a href="#cite_ref-Masters_38-0">\n           <sup>\n            <i>\n             <b>\n              a\n             </b>\n            </i>\n           </sup>\n          </a>\n          <a href="#cite_ref-Masters_38-1">\n           <sup>\n            <i>\n             <b>\n              b\n             </b>\n            </i>\n           </sup>\n          </a>\n          <a href="#cite_ref-Masters_38-2">\n           <sup>\n            <i>\n             <b>\n              c\n             </b>\n            </i>\n           </sup>\n          </a>\n         </span>\n         <span class="reference-text">\n          <cite class="citation web">\n           Masters, Jeff.\n           <a class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20121103064238/http://www.wunderground.com/blog/JeffMasters/comment.html?entrynum=2283" rel="nofollow">\n            "Why did Hurricane Sandy take such an unusual track into New Jersey?"\n           </a>\n           .
